jayati parāśara sūnuḥ satyavatī hṛdaya nandanaḥ vyāsaḥ yasya āsya kamala kośe vāc mayam amṛtam pibati lokaḥ dharma dṛḍha baddha mūlaḥ veda skandhaḥ purāṇa śākhā āḍhyaḥ pitāmaha ādyam pravadanti ṣaṣṭham mahā ṛṣim akṣayya vibhūti yuktam nārāyaṇasya aṃśa jam eka putram dvaipāyanam veda nidhim namāmi pārāśarya vacaḥ sarojam amalam gīta artha gandha utkaṭam nānā ākhyānaka kesaram hari kathā saṃbodhana ābodhitam loke sat jana ṣaṭpadaiḥ aharahar pepīyamānam mudā bhūyāt bhārata paṅkajam kali mala pradhvaṃsi naḥ śreyase yaḥ śveta tvam upāgataḥ kṛta yuge tretā yuge rakta tām yugme yaḥ kapilaḥ kalau ca bhagavān kṛṣṇa tvam āyāga vāgīśa ādyāḥ sumanasaḥ sarva arthānām tvā kṛtakṛtyāḥ syuḥ tam namāmi gajānanam vyāsam vasiṣṭha naptāram śakteḥ pautram akalmaṣam parāśara ātmajam vande śuka tātam tapas nidhim śambhuḥ bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ śukla ambara dharam devam śaśi varṇam catur bhujam jñāna ānanda mayam devam nirmalam sphaṭika ākṛtim ādhāram sarva vidyānām hayagrīvam upāsmahe vyāsāya viṣṇu rūpāya vyāsa rūpāya viṣṇave namaḥ dharmāya mahate namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase brāhmaṇebhyaḥ namaskṛtvā dharmān vakṣyāmi śāśvatān abhra śyāmaḥ piṅga jaṭā baddha kalāpaḥ prāṃśuḥ daṇḍī kṛṣṇa mṛga tvac paridhānaḥ sākṣāt lokān pāvayamānaḥ kavi mukhyaḥ pārāśaryaḥ parvasu rūpam vivṛṇotu aśubhāni nirācaṣṭe tanoti śubha saṃtatim smṛta mātreṇa yaḥ puṃsām brahma tat maṅgalam viduḥ pāpam praṇaśyati vṛkodara kīrtanena mādrī sutau kathayatām na bhavanti rogāḥ tviṣām patim gaṇapatim bṛhaspati mukhān ṛṣīn nārāyaṇam suragurum jagat eka nātham traiguṇya varjitam ajam vibhum ādyam īśam nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya naram ca eva narottamam lomaharṣaṇa putra ugraśravas sūta paurāṇika naimiṣa araṇya śaunaka kula pati dvādaśan vārṣika sattra samāsīnān abhyagacchat brahmarṣīn saṃśita vratān vinaya avanataḥ bhūtvā kadā cit sūtanandanaḥ tam āśramam anuprāptam naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ uvāca tān ṛṣīn sarvān dhanyaḥ vaḥ asmi adya darśanāt veda vaiyāsikīḥ sarvāḥ kathāḥ dharma artha saṃhitāḥ vakṣyāmi vaḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ śṛṇvantu adya tapodhanāḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ abhivādya munīn tān tu sarvān eva kṛtāñjaliḥ atha teṣu upaviṣṭeṣu sarveṣu eva tapasviṣu nirdiṣṭam āsanam bheje vinayāt lomaharṣaṇaḥ sukha āsīnam tatas tam tu viśrāntam upalakṣya ca atha apṛcchat ṛṣiḥ tatra kaḥ cit prastāvayan kathāḥ kālaḥ kamala pattra akṣa śaṃsa etat pṛcchataḥ mama evam pṛṣṭaḥ abravīt samyak yathāvat lomaharṣaṇaḥ vākyam vacana saṃpannaḥ teṣām tu carita āśrayam tasmin sadasi vistīrṇe munīnām bhāvitātmanām uvāca kṛṣṇadvaipāyana proktāḥ su puṇyāḥ vividhāḥ kathāḥ kathitāḥ ca api vidhivat yāḥ vaiśampāyanena vai śrutvā aham tāḥ vicitra arthāḥ mahābhārata saṃśritāḥ bahūni saṃparikramya tīrthāni āyatanāni ca samantapañcakam nāma puṇyam dvija niṣevitam gatavan asmi tam deśam yuddham yatra abhavat purā pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca sarveṣām ca mahīkṣitām didṛkṣuḥ āgataḥ tasmāt samīpam bhavatām iha āyuṣmantaḥ sarve eva brahma bhūtāḥ hi me matāḥ asmin yajñe mahābhāgāḥ sūrya pāvaka varcasaḥ kṛta abhiṣekāḥ śucayaḥ kṛta japyāḥ huta agnayaḥ purāṇa saṃśritāḥ puṇyāḥ kathāḥ vā dharma saṃśritāḥ itivṛttam narendrāṇām ṛṣīṇām ca mahātmanām śrutam mama bhārata ākhyānam dharma kāma artha mokṣa dam janamejayena pṛṣṭaḥ san vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uktavan ṛṣīṇām agratas tatra dharmiṣṭhānām mahātmanām vyāsa deva ājñayā tatra yat vaiśampāyanaḥ tadā śrutam vai bhārata ākhyānam veda arthaiḥ ca upabṛṃhitam tatra mama viditam sarvam bhārata ākhyānam āditas ūcuḥ dvaipāyanena yat proktam purāṇam parama ṛṣiṇā sūkṣma artha nyāya yuktasya veda arthaiḥ bhūṣitasya ca bhāratasya itihāsasya puṇyām grantha artha saṃyutām saṃskāra upagatām brāhmīm nānā śāstra upabṛṃhitām janamejayasya yām rājñaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uktavan yathāvat saḥ ṛṣiḥ tuṣṭyā satre dvaipāyana ājñayā vedaiḥ caturbhiḥ samitām vyāsasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ saṃhitām śrotum icchāmaḥ dharmyām pāpa bhaya apahām uvāca ādyam puruṣam īśānam puru hūtam puruṣṭutam ṛtam ekākṣaram brahma vyakta avyaktam sanātanam parāvarāṇām sraṣṭāram purāṇam param avyayam maṅgalyam maṅgalam viṣṇum vareṇyam anagham śucim namaskṛtya hṛṣīkeśam carācara gurum harim pravakṣyāmi matam kṛtsnam vyāsasya amita tejasaḥ yasya prasādāt vakṣyāmi nārāyaṇa kathām imām sarva āśrama abhigamanam sarva tīrtha avagāhanam na tathā phala dam sūte nārāyaṇa kathā yathā na asti nārāyaṇa samam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati idam tu triṣu lokeṣu mahat jñānam pratiṣṭhitam alaṃkṛtam śubhaiḥ śabdaiḥ samayaiḥ divya mānuṣaiḥ viśodhya deham dharma ātmā darbha saṃstaram āśritaḥ śuciḥ sa niyamaḥ vyāsaḥ śānta ātmā tapasi sthitaḥ bhāratasya itihāsasya dharmeṇa anvīkṣya tām gatim bṛhat aṇḍam abhūt ekam prajānām bījam akṣayam avyaktam kāraṇam sūkṣmam yat tat sat asat ātmakam brahmā suraguruḥ sthāṇuḥ manuḥ kaḥ parameṣṭhī atha tatas prajānām patayaḥ prābhavan ekaviṃśatiḥ puruṣaḥ ca aprameya ātmā yam sarvam ṛṣayaḥ viduḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā ādityāḥ vasavaḥ atha aśvinaḥ api yakṣāḥ sādhyāḥ piśācāḥ ca guhyakāḥ pitaraḥ tathā tatas prasūtāḥ vidvasaḥ śiṣṭāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ amalāḥ rājarṣayaḥ ca bahavaḥ sarvaiḥ samuditāḥ guṇaiḥ apaḥ dyauḥ pṛthivī vāyuḥ antarikṣam diśaḥ tathā saṃvatsara ṛtavaḥ māsāḥ pakṣa ahar rātrayaḥ kramāt kṣaṇāḥ lavāḥ muhūrtāḥ ca nimeṣāḥ yuga paryayāḥ yat ca anyat api tat sarvam saṃbhūtam loka sākṣikam yat idam dṛśyate kim cit bhūtam sthāvara jaṅgamam yathā ṛtau ṛtu liṅgāni nānā rūpāṇi paryaye dṛśyante tāni tāni eva tathā bhāvāḥ yuga ādiṣu evam etat anādi antam bhūta saṃhāra kārakam trayastriṃśat sahasrāṇi trayastriṃśat śatāni ca trayastriṃśat ca devānām sṛṣṭiḥ saṃkṣepa lakṣaṇā divasputraḥ bṛhadbhānuḥ cakṣuḥ ātmā vibhāvasuḥ savitā ca ṛcīkaḥ arkaḥ bhānuḥ āśāvahaḥ raviḥ putrāḥ vivasvantaḥ sarve mahyaḥ teṣām tathā avaraḥ devabhrāj tanayaḥ tasya tasmāt subhrāj iti smṛtaḥ subhrājaḥ tu trayaḥ putrāḥ prajāvantaḥ bahu śrutāḥ daśa putra sahasrāṇi daśajyoteḥ mahātmanaḥ tatas daśaguṇāḥ ca anye śatajyoteḥ iha ātmajāḥ bhūyas tatas daśaguṇāḥ sahasrajyotiṣaḥ sutāḥ tebhyaḥ ayam kuru vaṃśaḥ ca yadūnām bharatasya ca yayāti ikṣvāku vaṃśaḥ ca rājarṣīṇām ca sarvaśas saṃbhūtāḥ bahavaḥ vaṃśāḥ bhūta sargāḥ sa vistarāḥ bhūta sthānāni sarvāṇi rahasyam trividham ca yat veda yogam sa vijñānam dharmaḥ arthaḥ kāmaḥ eva ca dharma kāma artha śāstrāṇi śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca lokayātrā vidhānam ca saṃbhūtam dṛṣṭavan ṛṣiḥ itihāsāḥ sa vaiyākhyāḥ vividhāḥ śrutayaḥ api ca saṃkṣepeṇa itihāsasya tatas vakṣyāmi vistaram vistīrya etat mahat jñānam ṛṣiḥ saṃkṣepam abravīt iṣṭam hi viduṣām loke samāsa vyāsa dhāraṇam manu ādi bhāratam ke cid āstīka ādi tathā apare vividham saṃhitā jñānam dīpayanti manīṣiṇaḥ vyākhyātum kuśalāḥ ke cid grantham dhārayitum pare itihāsam imam cakre puṇyam satyavatī sutaḥ parāśara ātmajaḥ vidvān brahmarṣiḥ saṃśita vrataḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam vyāsam viddhi nārāyaṇam prabhum kaḥ hi anyaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣāt mahābhārata kṛt bhavet bhāti sarveṣu vedeṣu ratiḥ sarveṣu jantuṣu taraṇam sarva lokānām tasmāt bhāratam ucyate mātuḥ niyogāt dharma ātmā gāṅgeyasya ca dhīmataḥ kṣetre vicitra vīryasya kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ purā trīn agnīn iva kauravyān janayām āsa vīryavān utpādya dhṛtarāṣṭram ca pāṇḍum viduram eva ca jagāma tapase dhīmān punar eva āśramam prati teṣu jāteṣu vṛddheṣu gateṣu paramām gatim evam vai saṃgraha adhyāyaḥ pūrvam eva mahā ṛṣiṇā etad artham ca vihitaḥ saṃgrahaḥ ayam yathāśrutaḥ tat śrutvā sarvam ākhyātam loke jñāsyanti mānavāḥ abravīt bhāratam loke mānuṣe asmin mahān ṛṣiḥ janamejayena pṛṣṭaḥ san brāhmaṇaiḥ ca sahasraśas śaśāsa śiṣyam āsīnam vaiśaṃpāyanam antike sa sadasyaiḥ saha āsīnaḥ śrāvayām āsa bhāratam karma antareṣu yajñasya codyamānaḥ punar punar vistaram kuru vaṃśasya gāndhāryāḥ dharma śīla tām kṣattuḥ prajñām dhṛtim kuntyāḥ samyak dvaipāyanaḥ abravīt vāsudevasya māhātmyam pāṇḍavānām ca satyatām durvṛttam dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām uktavan bhagavān ṛṣiḥ idam śata sahasra ākhyam ślokānām puṇya karmaṇām upākhyānaiḥ saha jñeyam śrāvyam bhāratam uttamam caturviṃśati sāhasrām cakre bhārata saṃhitām upākhyānaiḥ vinā tāvat bhāratam procyate budhaiḥ tatas adhyardha śatam bhūyas saṃkṣepam kṛtavan ṛṣiḥ anukramaṇim adhyāyam vṛttāntānām sa parvaṇām sūtaḥ tasya ākhyāna variṣṭhasya kṛtvā dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ priya artham mahā ṛṣeḥ ca api lokānām hita kāmyayā tam dṛṣṭvā vismitaḥ bhūtvā prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ sthitaḥ hiraṇyagarbham āsīnam tasmin tu parama āsane parivṛtya āsana abhyāśe vāsaveyaḥ sthitaḥ nataḥ anujñātaḥ atha kṛṣṇaḥ tu brahmanā parameṣṭhinā niṣasāda āsana abhyāśe prīyamāṇaḥ su vismitaḥ uvāca sa mahā tejāḥ brahmānam parameṣṭhinam kṛtam mayā idam bhagavant kāvyam parama pūjitam sāṅga upaniṣadānām ca vedānām vistara kriyā itihāsa purāṇānām unmeṣam nimiṣam ca yat bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyat ca trividham kāla saṃjñitam jarā mṛtyu bhaya vyādhi bhāva abhāva viniścayam vividhasya ca dharmasya hi āśramāṇām ca lakṣaṇam cāturvarṇya vidhānam ca purāṇa artham ca kṛtsnaśas graha nakṣatra tārāṇām pramāṇam ca yugaiḥ saha ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni veda adhyātmam tathā eva ca nyāyaḥ śikṣā cikitsā ca jñānam pāśupatam tathā iti na eka āśrayam janma divya mānuṣa saṃśritam tīrthānām ca eva puṇyānām deśānām ca eva kīrtanam nadīnām parvatānām ca vanānām sāgarasya ca purāṇām ca eva divyānām kalpānām yuddha kauśalam vākya jāti viśeṣān ca lokayātrā kramaḥ ca yaḥ tapaḥ viśiṣṭāt api vai vasiṣṭhāt muni puṃgavāt manye śreṣṭhatamam tvā adya rahasya jñāna vedanāt janma prabhṛti satyām te vidma gām brahma vādinīm tvayā ca kāvyam iti uktam tasmāt kāvyam bhaviṣyati viśeṣaṇe gṛhasthasya śeṣāḥ trayaḥ iva āśramāḥ yadi jñāna hutāśena tvayā na ujjvalitam bhavet jñāna añjana śalākābhiḥ buddhi netra utsavaḥ kṛtaḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣa arthaiḥ samāsa vyāsa kīrtanaiḥ tvayā bhārata sūryeṇa nṛṇām vinihatam tamaḥ purāṇa pūrṇa candreṇa śruti jyotsnā prakāśiṇā nṛṇām kumuda saumyānām kṛtam buddhi prabodhanam itihāsa pradīpena moha āvaraṇa ghātinā loka garbhagṛham kṛtsnam yathāvat saṃprakāśitam saṃgraha adhyāya bījaḥ vai pauloma āstīka mūlavān saṃbhava skandha vistāraḥ sabhā araṇya viṭaṅkavān araṇī parva rūpa āḍhyaḥ virāṭa udyoga sāravān bhīṣmaparva mahā śākhaḥ droṇaparva palāśavān strīparva aiṣīka viśrāmaḥ śāntiparva bṛhat phalaḥ aśvamedha amṛta rasaḥ tu āśrama sthāna saṃśrayaḥ mausala śruti saṃkṣepaḥ śiṣṭa dvija niṣevitaḥ sarveṣām kavi mukhyānām upajīvyaḥ bhaviṣyati parjanyaḥ iva bhūtānām akṣayaḥ bhārata drumaḥ evam ābhāṣya tam brahmā jagāma svam niveśanam bhagavān sa jagatsraṣṭā ṛṣi deva gaṇaiḥ saha tasya vṛkṣasya vakṣyāmi śaśvat puṣpa phala udayam saṃhitāḥ taiḥ pṛthaktvena bhāratasya prakīrtitāḥ ṣaṣṭim śata sahasrāṇi cakāra anyām sa saṃhitām ekam śata sahasram tu mānuṣeṣu pratiṣṭhitam nāradaḥ aśrāvayat devān asitaḥ devalaḥ pitṝn gandharva yakṣa rakṣāṃsi śrāvayām āsa vai śukaḥ ismin tu mānuṣe loke vaiśampāyanaḥ uktavan śiṣyaḥ vyāsasya dharma ātmā sarva veda vidām varaḥ vaiśampāyana viprarṣiḥ śrāvayām āsa pārthivam pārikṣitam mahā bāhum nāmnā tu janamejayam duryodhanaḥ manyu mayaḥ mahā drumaḥ skandhaḥ karṇaḥ śakuniḥ tasya śākhāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ puṣpa phale samṛddhe mūlam rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ amanīṣī mādrī sutau puṣpa phale samṛddhe mūlam kṛṣṇaḥ brahma ca brāhmaṇāḥ ca pāṇḍuḥ jitvā bahūn deśān yudhā vikramaṇena ca araṇye mṛgayā śīlaḥ nyavasat sa janaḥ tadā mṛga vyavāya nidhane kṛcchrām prāpa saḥ āpadam janma prabhṛti pārthānām tatra ācāra vidhi kramaḥ dharmasya vāyoḥ śakrasya devayoḥ ca tathā aśvinoḥ tatas dharma upaniṣadam bhūtvā bhartuḥ priyā pṛthā dharma anila indrān tābhiḥ sā ājuhāva suta vāñchayā tad datta upaniṣad mādrī ca aśvinau ājuhāva ca jātāḥ pārthāḥ tatas sarve kuntyāḥ mādryāḥ ca mantratas teṣu jāteṣu sarveṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu mādryā tu saha saṃgamya ṛṣi śāpa prabhāvāt mṛtaḥ pāṇḍuḥ mahā puṇye śataśṛṅge mahā girau tāpasaiḥ saha saṃvṛddhāḥ mātṛbhyām parirakṣitāḥ medhya araṇyeṣu puṇyeṣu mahatām āśrameṣu ca ṛṣibhiḥ ca tadā ānītāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān prati svayam śiśavaḥ ca abhirūpāḥ ca jaṭilāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ putrāḥ ca bhrātaraḥ ca ime śiṣyāḥ ca suhṛdaḥ ca vaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ete iti uktvā munayaḥ antarhitāḥ tatas tān taiḥ niveditān dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavān kauravāḥ tadā śiṣṭāḥ ca varṇāḥ paurāḥ ye te harṣāt cukruśuḥ bhṛśam yadā cira mṛtaḥ pāṇḍuḥ katham tasya iti ca apare svāgatam sarvathā diṣṭyā pāṇḍoḥ paśyāma saṃtatim ucyatām svāgatam iti vācaḥ aśrūyanta sarvaśas antarhitānām bhūtānām nisvanaḥ tumulaḥ abhavat puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ śubha gandhāḥ śaṅkha dundubhi nisvanāḥ āsan praveśe pārthānām tat adbhutam iva abhavat tad prītyā ca eva sarveṣām paurāṇām harṣa saṃbhavaḥ śabdaḥ āsīt mahān tatra diva kīrti vardhanaḥ te api adhītya akhilān vedān śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca nyavasan pāṇḍavāḥ tatra pūjitāḥ akutobhayāḥ yudhiṣṭhirasya śaucena prītāḥ prakṛtayaḥ abhavan guru śuśrūṣayā kuntyāḥ yamayoḥ vinayena ca tutoṣa lokaḥ sakalaḥ teṣām śaurya guṇena ca samavāye tatas rājñām kanyām bhartṛ svayaṃvarām prāptavan arjunaḥ kṛṣṇām kṛtvā karma su duṣkaram ādityaḥ iva duṣprekṣyaḥ samareṣu api ca abhavat sa sarvān pārthivān jitvā sarvān ca mahataḥ gaṇān ājahāra arjunaḥ rājñe rājasūyam mahā kratum annavān dakṣiṇāvān ca sarvaiḥ samuditaḥ guṇaiḥ yudhiṣṭhireṇa saṃprāptaḥ rājasūyaḥ mahā kratuḥ maṇi kāñcana ratnāni go hasti aśva dhanāni ca vicitrāṇi ca vāsāṃsi prāvāra āvaraṇāni ca kambala ajina ratnāni rāṅkava āstaraṇāni ca samṛddhām tām tathā dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānām tadā śriyam īrṣyā samutthaḥ su mahān tasya manyuḥ ajāyata vimāna pratimām ca api mayena su kṛtām sabhām pāṇḍavānām upahṛtām sa dṛṣṭvā paryatapyata kathitaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya vivarṇaḥ hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ anvajānāt tatas dyūtam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ suta priyaḥ na ati prīta manāḥ ca āsīt vivādān ca anvamodata dyūta ādīn anayān ghorān pravṛddhān ca api upaikṣata nirasya viduram droṇam bhīṣmam śāradvatam kṛpam jayatsu pāṇḍu putreṣu śrutvā su mahat apriyam duryodhana matam jñātvā karṇasya śakuneḥ tathā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ciram dhyātvā saṃjayam vākyam abravīt śṛṇu saṃjaya mama sarvam na me asūyitum arhasi śrutavān asi medhāvī buddhimān prājña saṃmataḥ na me viśeṣaḥ putreṣu sveṣu pāṇḍu suteṣu ca vṛddham mām abhyasūyanti putrāḥ manyu parāyaṇāḥ aham tu acakṣuḥ kārpaṇyāt putra prītyā sahāmi tat rājasūye śriyam dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavasya mahat ojas tat ca avahasanam prāpya sabhā rohaṇa darśane amarṣitaḥ svayam jetum aśaktaḥ pāṇḍavān raṇe nirutsāhaḥ ca saṃprāptum śriyam a kṣatriyaḥ yathā tatra yat yat yathā jñātam mayā saṃjaya tat śṛṇu śrutvā hi mama vākyāni buddhyā yuktāni tattvataḥ tatas jñāsyasi mām saute prajñācakṣuṣam iti uta yadā aśrauṣam dhanuḥ āyamya citram viddham lakṣyam pātitam vai pṛthivyām kṛṣṇām hṛ paśyatām sarva rājñām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam dvārakāyām subhadrām prasahya ūḍhām mādhavīm arjunena indraprastham vṛṣṇi vīrau ca yātau tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam devarājam pravṛṣṭam śaraiḥ divyaiḥ vāritam ca arjunena agnim tathā tarpitam khāṇḍave ca tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam jātuṣāt veśmanaḥ tān muktān pārthān pañca kuntyā sametān yuktam ca eṣām viduram sva artha siddhyai tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam draupadīm raṅga madhye śūrān pāñcālān pāṇḍaveyān ca yuktān tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam māgadhānām variṣṭham dorbhyām hatam bhīmasenena gatvā tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam digjaye pāṇḍu putraiḥ vaśīkṛtān bhūmipālān prasahya mahā kratum rājasūyam kṛtam ca tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam sarva viśvasya prītyā rājñe nirmitām tām mayena gadām ca ugrām bhīmasenāya dattām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam hṛta rājyam yudhiṣṭhiram parājitam saubalena akṣavatyām anvāgatam bhrātṛbhiḥ aprameyaiḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam draupadīm aśru kaṇṭhīm sabhām nītām duḥkhitām eka vastrām rajasvalām nāthavatīm anātha vat tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāsasām tatra rāśim duḥśāsanaḥ gatavan na eva ca antam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vividhāḥ tāta ceṣṭāḥ dharma ātmanām prasthitānām vanāya jyeṣṭha prītyā kliśyatām pāṇḍavānām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam draupadīm tām bruvāṇām pravrajyāyām aśru kaṇṭhīm rudantīm tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam snātakānām sahasraiḥ anvāgatam dharmarājam vanastham bhikṣā bhujām brāhmaṇānām mahātmanām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vana vāseṣu pārthān samāgatān ṛṣi mukhyaiḥ purāṇaiḥ upāsyamānān sa gaṇaiḥ jātu sarvān tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam arjunaḥ devadevam kirāta rūpam tryambakam toṣya yuddhe avāpa tat pāśupatam mahā astram tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam tridiva stham dhanaṃjayam śakrāt sākṣāt divyam astram yathāvat adhīyānam śaṃsitam satya saṃdham tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam kālakeyāḥ tatas te paulomānaḥ vara dattāḥ ca dṛptāḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam asurāṇām vadha artham kirīṭinam yātam amitra karṣaṇam kṛtārtham ca api āgatam śakra lokāt tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam tīrtha yātrā pravṛttam pāṇḍoḥ sutam sahitam romaśena tasmāt śrutam ca arjunasya astra lābham tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vaiśravaṇena sārdham samāgatam bhīmam anyān ca pārthān tasmin deśe mānuṣāṇām agamye tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam ghoṣa yātrā gatānām bandham gandharvaiḥ mokṣaṇam ca arjunena svānām sutānām karṇa buddhau ratānām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam draupadīm saindhavena na ānītām mokṣitām ca arjunena jayadratham mokṣitam jīva śeṣam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam yakṣa rūpeṇa dharmam samāgatam dharmarājena sūta praśnān uktān vibruvantam ca samyak tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam na viduḥ māmakāḥ tān pracchanna rūpān vasataḥ pāṇḍaveyān virāṭa rāṣṭre saha kṛṣṇayā tān tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam tān atha ajñāta vāse tu apaśyamānān vividhaiḥ upāyaiḥ dakṣān pārthān me sutaiḥ agni kalpān tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam kīcakānām variṣṭham niṣūditam bhrātṛ śatena sārdham tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vasataḥ pāṇḍu putrān adṛśyamānān vividhaiḥ upāyaiḥ dakṣān pārthān bhīmasenena saṃkhye tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam māmakānām variṣṭhān dhanaṃjayena eka rathena bhagnān virāṭa rāṣṭre vasatā mahātmanā tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam satkṛtām matsya rājñā sutām dattām uttarām arjunāya tām ca arjunaḥ pratyagṛhṇāt suta arthe tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta yudhiṣṭhirasya tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam nara nārāyaṇau tau kṛṣṇa arjunau vadataḥ nāradasya aham draṣṭā brahma loke sadā iti tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam mādhavam vāsudevam sarva ātmanā pāṇḍava arthe niviṣṭam yasya imām gām vikramam ekam āhuḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam loka hitāya kṛṣṇam śama arthinam upayātam kurūṇām śamam kurvāṇam akṛtārtham ca yātam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇa duryodhanābhyām buddhim kṛtām nigrahe keśavasya tam ca ātmānam bahudhā darśayānam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāsudeve prayāte rathasya ekām agratas sthamānām ārtām pṛthām sāntvitām keśavena tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāsudeve prayāte tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam mantriṇam vāsudevam tathā bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam ca teṣām bhāradvājam ca āśiṣaḥ anubruvāṇam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇaḥ uvāca bhīṣmam na aham yotsye yudhyamāne tvayi iti hitvā senām apacakrāma ca eva tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāsudeva arjunau tau tathā dhanuḥ gāṇḍivam aprameyam trīṇi ugra vīryāṇi samāgatāni tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya kṛṣṇam lokān darśayānam śarīre tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam bhīṣmam amitra karśanam nighnantam ājau ayutam rathānām na eṣām kaḥ cit vadhyate dṛśya rūpaḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam ca āpageyena saṃkhye svayam mṛtyum vihitam dhārmikeṇa tat ca akārṣuḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam bhīṣmam atyanta śūram hatam pārthena āhaveṣu apradhṛṣyam śikhaṇḍinam puratas sthāpayitvā tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śara talpe śayānam vṛddham vīram sāditam citrapuṅkhaiḥ bhīṣmam kṛtvā somakān alpa śeṣān tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śāṃtanave śayāne pānīya arthe ca uditena arjunena bhūmim bhittvā tarpitam tatra bhīṣmam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śukra sūryau ca yuktau kaunteyānām anulomau jayāya nityam ca asmān śvāpadāḥ vyābhaṣantaḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya na pāṇḍavān śreṣṭhatamān nihanti tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam ca asmadīyān mahā rathān vyavasthitān arjunasya antakāya saṃśaptakān nihatān arjunena tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vyūham abhedyam anyaiḥ bhāradvājena ātta śastreṇa guptam bhittvā saubhadram vīram ekam praviṣṭam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā abhimanyum parivārya bālam sarve hatvā hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ babhūvuḥ mahā rathāḥ pārtham aśaknuvantaḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam abhimanyum nihatya harṣāt mūḍhān krośataḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān krodham muktam saindhave ca arjunena tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam saindhava arthe pratijñām pratijñātām tad vadhāya arjunena satyām nistīrṇām śatru madhye ca tena yadā aśrauṣam śrānta haye dhanaṃjaye muktvā hayān pāyayitvā upavṛttān punar yuktvā vāsudevam prayātam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāhaneṣu āśvasatsu rathopasthe tiṣṭhatā gāṇḍivena sarvān yodhān vāritān arjunena tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam nāga balaiḥ durutsaham droṇa anīkam yuyudhānam pramathya yātam vārṣṇeyam yatra tau kṛṣṇa pārthau tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇam āsādya muktam vadhāt bhīmam kutsayitvā vacobhiḥ dhanuṣkoṭyā tudya karṇena vīram tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā droṇaḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ ca karṇaḥ drauṇiḥ madra rājaḥ ca śūraḥ amarṣayan saindhavam vadhyamānam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam devarājena dattām divyām śaktim vyaṃsitām mādhavena ghaṭotkace rākṣase ghora rūpe tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇa ghaṭotkacābhyām yuddhe muktām sūtaputreṇa śaktim yad vadhyaḥ samare savyasācī tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam droṇam ācāryam ekam dhṛṣṭadyumnena abhyatikramya dharmam rathopasthe prāya gatam viśastam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam drauṇinā dvairatha stham mādrī putram nakulam loka madhye samam yuddhe pāṇḍavam yudhyamānam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya na eṣām antam gatavan pāṇḍavānām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam bhīmasenena pītam raktam bhrātuḥ yudhi duḥśāsanasya nivāritam na anyatamena bhīmam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam bhīma karmāṇam ugram raṇe bhīmam śoṇitam pītavantam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇam atyanta śūram hatam pārthena āhaveṣu apradhṛṣyam tasmin bhrātṝṇām vigrahe deva guhye tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam droṇaputram kṛpam ca duḥśāsanam kṛtavarmāṇam ugram yudhiṣṭhiram śūnyam a dharṣayantam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam nihatam madra rājam raṇe śūram dharmarājena sūta sadā saṃgrāme spardhate yaḥ sa kṛṣṇam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam kalaha dyūta mūlam māyā balam saubalam pāṇḍavena hatam saṃgrāme sahadevena pāpam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śrāntam ekam śayānam hradam gatvā stambhayitvā tat ambhaḥ duryodhanam viratham bhagna darpam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam pāṇḍavān tiṣṭhamānān gaṅgāhrade vāsudevena sārdham amarṣaṇam dharṣayataḥ sutam mama tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vividhān tāta mārgān gadā yuddhe maṇḍalam saṃcarantam mithyā hatam vāsudevasya buddhyā tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam droṇaputra ādibhiḥ taiḥ hatān pāñcālān draupadeyān ca suptān kṛtam bībhatsam ayaśasyam ca karma tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam bhīmasena anuyātena aśvatthāmnā parama astram prayuktam kruddhena aiṣīkam avadhīt yena garbham tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam brahmaśiraḥ arjunena muktam svasti iti astram astreṇa śāntam aśvatthāmnā maṇi ratnam ca dattam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam droṇaputreṇa garbhe vairāṭyāḥ vai pātyamāne mahā astre saṃjīvayāmi iti hareḥ pratijñām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya dvaipāyanaḥ keśavaḥ droṇaputram paraspareṇa abhiśāpaiḥ śaśāpa buddhvā ca aham buddhi hīnaḥ adya sūta saṃtapye aham putra pautraiḥ ca hīnaḥ kartavyatām na abhijānāmi sūta śocyā gāndhārī putra pautraiḥ vihīnā tathā vadhvaḥ pitṛbhiḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ ca kṛ kāryam duṣkaram pāṇḍaveyaiḥ prāptam rājyam asapatnam punar taiḥ kaṣṭa yuddha daśan śeṣa śru mad tri mad pāṇḍavānām ca saptan dvi ūnāḥ viṃśatiḥ āhata akṣauhiṇīnām tasmin saṃgrāme vigrahe kṣatriyāṇām kāla abhipannā samitiḥ mahātmanām niṣūditā hetuḥ āsīt sutaḥ me tamasā tu abhyavastīrṇaḥ mohaḥ āviśati iva mām saṃjñām na upalabhe sūta manaḥ vihvalati iva mama iti uktvā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ atha vilapya bahu duḥkhitaḥ mūrcchitaḥ punar āśvastaḥ saṃjayam vākyam abravīt saṃjaya evaṃgate prāṇān tyaktum icchāmi māciram stokam hi api na paśyāmi phalam jīvita dhāraṇe tam tathāvādinam dīnam vilapantam mahīpatim niḥśvasantam yathā nāgam muhyamānam punar punar gāvalgaṇiḥ idam dhīmān mahā artham vākyam abravīt śrutavān asi vai rājñaḥ mahā utsāhān mahā balān mahatsu rāja vaṃśeṣu guṇaiḥ samuditeṣu ca jātān divya astra viduṣaḥ śakra pratima tejasaḥ dharmeṇa pṛthivīm jitvā yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā āpta dakṣiṇaiḥ asmin loke yaśaḥ prāpya tatas kāla vaśam gatāḥ vainyam mahā ratham vīram sṛñjayam jayatām varam vāhlīkam damanam śaibyam śaryātim ajitam jitam rāmam dāśarathim ca eva śaśabindum bhagīratham kṛtavīryam mahābhāgam tathā eva janamejayam yayātim śubha karmāṇam devaiḥ yaḥ yājitaḥ svayam caitya yūpa aṅkitā bhūmiḥ yasya iyam savana ākarā iti rājñām caturviṃśat nāradena sura ṛṣiṇā putra śoka abhitaptāya purā śaibyāya kīrtitāḥ tebhyaḥ ca anye gatāḥ pūrvam rājānaḥ balavattarāḥ mahā rathāḥ mahātmānaḥ sarvaiḥ samuditāḥ guṇaiḥ pūruḥ kuruḥ yaduḥ śūraḥ viṣvagaśvaḥ mahādhṛtiḥ anenāḥ yuvanāśvaḥ ca kakutsthaḥ vikramī raghuḥ vijitī vītihotraḥ ca bhavaḥ śvetaḥ bṛhadguruḥ uśīnaraḥ śatarathaḥ kaṅkaḥ duliduhaḥ drumaḥ ajeyaḥ paraśuḥ puṇḍraḥ śambhuḥ devāvṛdhaḥ anaghaḥ mahā utsāhaḥ vinīta ātmā sukratuḥ naiṣadhaḥ nalaḥ satyavrataḥ śāntabhayaḥ sumitraḥ subalaḥ prabhuḥ jānujaṅghaḥ anaraṇyaḥ arkaḥ priya bhṛtyaḥ śubha vrataḥ balabandhuḥ nirāmardaḥ ketuśṛṅgaḥ bṛhat balaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ bṛhatketuḥ dīptaketuḥ nirāmayaḥ avikṣit prabalaḥ dhūrtaḥ kṛtabandhuḥ dṛḍheṣudhiḥ mahā purāṇaḥ saṃbhāvyaḥ pratyaṅgaḥ para hā śrutiḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas śrūyante ayutaśas ca anye saṃkhyātāḥ ca api padmaśas rājānaḥ nidhanam prāptāḥ tava putraiḥ mahattamāḥ yeṣām divyāni karmāṇi vikramaḥ tyāgaḥ eva ca māhātmyam api ca āstikyam satyatā śaucam ārjavam sarva ṛddhi guṇa saṃpannāḥ te ca api nidhanam gatāḥ tava putrāḥ durātmānaḥ prataptāḥ ca eva manyunā lubdhāḥ durvṛtta bhūyiṣṭhāḥ na tān śocitum arhasi śrutavān asi medhāvī buddhimān prājña saṃmataḥ yeṣām śāstra anugā buddhiḥ na te muhyanti bhārata na atyantam eva anuvṛttiḥ śrūyate putra rakṣaṇe daivam prajñā viśeṣeṇa kaḥ nivartitum arhati vidhātṛ vihitam mārgam na kaḥ cit ativartate kāla mūlam idam sarvam bhāva abhāvau sukha asukhe kālaḥ pacati bhūtāni kālaḥ saṃharati prajāḥ nirdahantam prajāḥ kālam kālaḥ śamayate punar kālaḥ vikurute bhāvān sarvān loke śubha aśubhān kālaḥ saṃkṣipate sarvāḥ prajāḥ visṛjate punar kālaḥ supteṣu jāgarti kālaḥ hi duratikramaḥ uvāca atītān āgatān vā api vartamānāḥ tathā budhāḥ kālaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu carati a vidhṛtaḥ samaḥ atīta anāgatāḥ bhāvāḥ ye ca vartanti sāṃpratam tān kāla nirmitān buddhvā na saṃjñām hātum arhasi iti evam putra śoka ārtam dhṛtarāṣṭram janeśvaram āśvāsya svastham akarot sūtaḥ gāvalgaṇiḥ tadā evam uktvā ca rājānam saṃjayaḥ virarāma ha dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ api tat śrutvā dhṛtim eva samāśrayat diṣṭyā idam āgatam iti matvā sa prājña sattamaḥ uvāca atra upaniṣadam puṇyām kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ abravīt bhārata adhyayanāt puṇyāt api pādam adhīyataḥ śraddadhānasya pūyante sarva pāpāni aśeṣatas lokānām ca hita arthāya kāruṇyāt muni sattamaḥ kīrtyante śubha karmāṇaḥ tathā yakṣa mahā uragāḥ bhagavant vāsudevaḥ ca kīrtyate atra sanātanaḥ śāśvatam brahma paramam dhruvam jyotiḥ sanātanam yasya divyāni karmāṇi kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ saṃtatiḥ ca pravṛttiḥ ca janma mṛtyuḥ punarbhavaḥ adhyātmam śrūyate yat ca pañca bhūta guṇa ātmakam yat tat yati varāḥ yuktāḥ dhyāna yoga bala anvitāḥ śraddadhānaḥ sadā udyuktaḥ satya dharma parāyaṇaḥ āsevan imam adhyāyam naraḥ pāpāt pramucyate anukramaṇim adhyāyam bhāratasya imam āditas āstikaḥ satatam śṛṇvan na kṛcchreṣu avasīdati anukramaṇyā yāvat syāt ahnā rātryā ca saṃcitam divyāḥ yajñāḥ ca nikhilā viṣṇuḥ ca upaniṣad mahat āraṇyakam ca vedebhyaḥ oṣadhibhyaḥ amṛtam yathā navanītam yathā dadhnaḥ dvipadām brāhmaṇaḥ yathā hradānām udadhiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ gauḥ variṣṭhā catuṣpadām yathā etāni variṣṭhāni tathā bhāratam ucyate yaḥ ca enam śrāvayet śrāddhe brāhmaṇān pādam antatas akṣayyam anna pānam tat pitṝn tasya upatiṣṭhati itihāsa purāṇābhyām vedam samupabṛṃhayet kārṣṇam vedam imam vidvān śrāvayitvā artham aśnute bhrūṇahatyā kṛtam ca api pāpam jahyāt na saṃśayaḥ yaḥ imam śuciḥ adhyāyam paṭhet parvaṇi parvaṇi adhītam bhāratam tena kṛtsnam syāt iti me matiḥ yaḥ ca imam śṛṇuyāt nityam ārṣam śraddhā samanvitaḥ sa dīrgham āyuḥ kīrtim ca svargatim ca āpnuyāt naraḥ samāgataiḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ tulām āropitam purā sūtaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam vyāsam viddhi nārāyaṇam vibhum kaḥ hi anyaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣāt mahābhārata kṛt bhavet stutyam tasya asti kim ca anyat sarvaloka hita eṣiṇaḥ vedāḥ vyastāḥ kṛtam tena mahābhāratam adbhutam iti uktvā sarva veda arthān bhārate tena darśitāḥ śrūyatām siṃhanādaḥ ayam ṛṣabhasya mahātmanaḥ varṇayeta katham dhīmān mahā kāruṇikaḥ muniḥ loka cintā avatāra artham varṇayitvā ca tena tau tulya arthāḥ saṃhitām puṇyām yojayiṣye tu tām aham tat ślokān ca samuddhartum kaḥ kṛtsnān bhārate kṣamaḥ kim tu bhārata bhaktiḥ mām vivaśam samacūcudat ūcuḥ uvāca śuśrūṣā yadi vaḥ viprāḥ bruvataḥ ca kathāḥ śubhāḥ tretā dvāparayoḥ saṃdhau rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ asakṛt pārthivam kṣatram jaghāna amarṣa coditaḥ sa sarvam kṣatram utsādya sva vīryeṇa anala dyutiḥ avistīrṇān jāmadagnyaḥ pratāpavān pitṝn saṃtarpayām āsa rudhireṇa iti naḥ śrutam uvāca rāma rāma mahābhāga prītāḥ sma te bhārgava varam vṛṇīṣva bhadram te kim icchasi mahā dyute yat ca roṣa abhibhūtena kṣatram utsāditam mayā atas ca pāpāt mucya iham eṣa me prārthitaḥ varaḥ hradāḥ ca tīrtha bhūtāḥ mama bhaveyuḥ bhuvi viśrutāḥ evam bhaviṣyati iti āh pitṛ brāhmaṇa ṛṣabha teṣām samīpe yaḥ deśaḥ hradānām rudhira ambhasām tena eva nāmnā tam deśam vācyam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ samantapañcake yuddham kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ aṣṭādaśa samājagmuḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ yuyutsayā sametya tam dvijāḥ tāḥ ca tatra eva nidhanam gatāḥ evam nāma abhinirvṛttam tasya deśasya vai dvijāḥ puṇyaḥ ca ramaṇīyaḥ ca sa deśaḥ vaḥ prakīrtitaḥ yathā deśaḥ sa vikhyātaḥ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ ūcuḥ akṣauhiṇyāḥ parīmāṇam ratha aśva nara dantinām uvāca ekaḥ rathaḥ gajaḥ ca ekaḥ narāḥ pañca padātayaḥ pattim tu triguṇām etām āhuḥ senāmukham budhāḥ trayaḥ gulmāḥ gaṇaḥ nāma vāhinī tu gaṇāḥ trayaḥ smṛtāḥ tisraḥ tu vāhinyaḥ pṛtanā iti vicakṣaṇaiḥ anīkinīm daśa guṇām prāhuḥ akṣauhiṇīm budhāḥ akṣauhiṇyāḥ prasaṃkhyānam rathānām dvijasattamāḥ saṃkhyā gaṇita tattva jñaiḥ sahasrāṇi ekaviṃśatiḥ śatāni upari ca eva aṣṭau tathā bhūyas ca saptatiḥ gajānām tu parīmāṇam etat eva atra nirdiśet jñeyam śata sahasram tu sahasrāṇi tathā nava narāṇām api pañcāśat śatāni trīṇi ca anaghāḥ pañca ṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi tathā aśvānām śatāni ca daśa uttarāṇi ṣaḍ prāhuḥ yathāvat iha saṃkhyayā etām akṣauhiṇīm prāhuḥ saṃkhyā tattva vidaḥ janāḥ yām vaḥ kathitavan asmi vistareṇa dvijottamāḥ etayā saṃkhyayā hi āsan kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ piṇḍena aṣṭādaśā eva tāḥ kauravān kāraṇam kṛtvā kālena adbhuta karmaṇā ahāni pañca droṇaḥ tu rarakṣa kuru vāhinīm kathitam vistara artham ca yaśaḥ vīryam mahīkṣitām ākhyānam kathitam kṛtsnam mahābhāratam uttamam ākhyāsye tatra paulomam ākhyānam ca āditas param abhipannam naraiḥ prājñaiḥ vairāgyam iva mokṣibhiḥ itihāsaḥ pradhāna arthaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarva āgameṣu ayam svara vyañjanayoḥ kṛtsnā loka veda āśrayā iva vāc bhāratasya itihāsasya śrūyatām parva saṃgrahaḥ ādiparva purā proktam pārāśaryeṇa dhīmatā parvan anukramaṇī pūrvam dvitīyam parvan saṃgrahaḥ pauṣyam paulomam āstīkam ādi vaṃśa avatāraṇam tatas svayaṃvaram devyāḥ pāñcālyāḥ parva ca ucyate arjunasya vane vāsaḥ subhadrā haraṇam tatas subhadrā haraṇāt ūrdhvam jñeyam haraṇahārikam tatas khāṇḍava dāha ākhyam tatra eva maya darśanam tatas ca argha abhiharaṇam śiśupāla vadhaḥ tatas īśvara arjunayoḥ yuddham parva kairāta saṃjñitam tīrtha yātrā tatas parva kururājasya dhīmataḥ saṃvādaḥ ca tatas parva draupadī satyabhāmayoḥ ghoṣa yātrā tatas parva mṛga svapna bhayam tatas rāma ākhyānam tatas parva sāvitrī ākhyānam eva ca pativratāyāḥ māhātmyam sāvitryāḥ ca evam adbhutam kuṇḍala āharaṇam parva tatas param iha ucyate āraṇeyam tatas parva vairāṭam tad anantaram pāṇḍavānām praveśaḥ ca samayasya ca pālanam kīcakānām vadhaḥ parva parva go grahaṇam tatas abhimanyunā ca vairāṭyāḥ parva vaivāhikam smṛtam tatas saṃjaya yāna ākhyam parva jñeyam atas param prajāgaram tatas parva dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cintayā mātalīyam upākhyānam caritam gālavasya ca jāmadagnyam upākhyānam parva ṣoḍaśa rājakam sabhā praveśaḥ kṛṣṇasya vidulā putra śāsanam udyogaḥ sainya niryāṇam śveta upākhyānam eva ca jñeyam vivāda parva atra karṇasya api mahātmanaḥ kīrtyate ca api upākhyānam saināpatye abhiṣecanam niryāṇam parva ca tatas kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ ulūka dūta āgamanam parva āmarṣa vivardhanam divyam cakṣuḥ dadau yatra saṃjayāya mahān ṛṣiḥ bhīṣma abhiṣecanam parva jñeyam adbhuta kāraṇam jambūkhaṇḍa vinirmāṇam parva uktam tad anantaram droṇa abhiṣekaḥ parva uktam saṃśaptaka vadhaḥ tatas mokṣaḥ nārāyaṇa astrasya parva anantaram ucyate sārasvatam tatas parva tīrtha vaṃśa guṇa anvitam aiṣīkam parva nirdiṣṭam atas ūrdhvam su dāruṇam śrāddha parva tatas jñeyam kurūṇām aurdhvadehikam ābhiṣecanikam parva dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ cārvāka nigrahaḥ parva rakṣasaḥ brahma rūpiṇaḥ pravibhāgaḥ gṛhānām ca parva uktam tad anantaram śuka praśna abhigamanam brahma praśna anuśāsanam prādurbhāvaḥ ca durvāsaḥ saṃvādaḥ ca eva māyayā tatas parva parijñeyam ānuśāsanikam param svarga ārohaṇikam parva tatas bhīṣmasya dhīmataḥ tatas aśvamedhikam parva sarva pāpa praṇāśanam anugītā tatas parva jñeyam adhyātma vācakam parva ca āśrama vāsa ākhyam putra darśanam eva ca varṇa dharmaḥ tatas jñeyam āśramāṇām ca kīrtanam mṛtānām darśanam ca eva vyāsena adbhuta karmaṇā mahāprasthānikam parva svarga ārohaṇikam tatas harivaṃśaḥ tatas parva purāṇam khila saṃjñitam viṣṇu parva śiśoḥ caryā viṣṇoḥ kaṃsa vadhaḥ tathā etat parva śatam pūrṇam vyāsena uktam mahātmanā yathāvat sūtaputreṇa lomaharṣaṇinā punar kathitam naimiṣa araṇye parvāṇi aṣṭādaśa eva tu samāsaḥ bhāratasya ayam tatra uktaḥ parva saṃgrahaḥ pauṣyam paulomam āstīkam ādi vaṃśa avatāraṇam tathā caitraratham devyāḥ pāñcālyāḥ ca svayaṃvaraḥ vana vāsaḥ arjunasya api subhadrā haraṇam tatas haraṇa āharaṇam ca eva dahanam khāṇḍavasya ca paulome bhṛgu vaṃśasya vistāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ślokānām ca sahasram ca pañcāśat śatam eva ca adhyāyānām tathā aṣṭau ca parvaṇi asmin prakīrtitāḥ āstīke sarva nāgānām garuḍasya ca saṃbhavaḥ yajataḥ sarpa satreṇa rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya ca kathā iyam abhinirvṛttā bhāratānām mahātmanām śloka agram ca sahasram ca tri śatam ca uttaram tathā ślokāḥ ca parvaṇi asmin tathā eva ca adhyāyānām tatas proktam catvāriṃśat mahā ṛṣiṇā vividhāḥ saṃbhavāḥ rājñām uktāḥ saṃbhava parvaṇi anyeṣām ca eva viprāṇām ṛṣeḥ dvaipāyanasya ca aṃśāvataraṇam ca atra devānām parikīrtitam daityānām dānavānām ca yakṣāṇām ca mahā ojasām nāgānām atha sarpāṇām gandharvāṇām patatriṇām anyeṣām ca eva bhūtānām vividhānām samudbhavaḥ śakuntalāyām duṣyantāt bharataḥ ca api jajñivān vasūnām punar utpattiḥ bhāgīrathyām mahātmanām śaṃtanoḥ veśmani punar teṣām ca ārohaṇam divi tejaḥ oṃśānām ca saṃghātāt bhīṣmasya api atra saṃbhavaḥ pratijñā pālanam ca eva rakṣā citrāṅgadasya ca hate citrāṅgade ca eva rakṣā bhrātuḥ yavīyasaḥ dharmasya nṛṣu saṃbhūtiḥ aṇīmāṇḍavya śāpa jā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt ca eva prasūtiḥ vara dāna jā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya pāṇḍoḥ ca pāṇḍavānām ca saṃbhavaḥ vidureṇa kṛtaḥ yatra hita artham mleccha bhāṣayā niṣādyāḥ pañca putrāyāḥ suptāyāḥ jatu veśmani pāṇḍavānām vane ghore hiḍimbāyāḥ ca darśanam tad ājñayā ekacakrāyām brāhmaṇasya niveśane a jñāta caryā pāṇḍūnām vāsaḥ brāhmaṇa veśmani bakasya nidhanam ca eva nāgarāṇām ca vismayaḥ saṃbhavaḥ ca eva kṛṣṇāyāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca eva ha brāhmaṇāt samupaśrutya vyāsa vākya pracoditāḥ draupadīm prārthayantaḥ te svayaṃvara didṛkṣavaḥ pāñcālān abhitas jagmuḥ yatra kautūhala anvitāḥ kūṭasya dhārtarāṣṭreṇa preṣaṇam pāṇḍavān prati aṅgāraparṇam nirjitya gaṅgā kūle arjunaḥ tadā sakhyam kṛtvā tatas tena tasmāt eva sa śuśruve bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ pāñcālān abhitas yayau tāpatyam atha vāsiṣṭham aurvam ca ākhyānam uttamam pāñcāla nagare ca api lakṣyam bhittvā dhanaṃjayaḥ bhīmasena arjunau yatra saṃrabdhān pṛthivīpatīn dṛṣṭvā tayoḥ ca tat vīryam aprameyam amānuṣam śaṅkamānau pāṇḍavān tān rāma kṛṣṇau mahā matī jagmatuḥ taiḥ samāgantum śālām bhārgava veśmani svayaṃvaram ca pāñcālyāḥ nṛpāṇām saha saṃgrāmaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā adbhutam pañca indrāṇām upākhyānam atra eva adbhutam ucyate draupadyāḥ deva vihitaḥ vivāhaḥ ca api amānuṣaḥ kṣattuḥ ca dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa preṣaṇam pāṇḍavān prati khāṇḍavaprastha vāsaḥ ca tathā rājya ardha śāsanam nāradasya ājñayā ca eva draupadyāḥ samayakriyā anantaram ca draupadyā saha āsīnam yudhiṣṭhiram mokṣayitvā gṛham gatvā vipra artham kṛta niścayaḥ pārthasya vana vāsaḥ ca ulūpyā pathi saṃgamaḥ puṇya tīrtha anusaṃyānam babhruvāhana janma ca tatra eva mokṣayām āsa pañca saḥ apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ śāpāt grāha tvam āpannāḥ brāhmaṇasya tapasvinaḥ prabhāsa tīrthe pārthasya kṛṣṇena ca samāgamaḥ dvārakāyām subhadrā ca kāmayānena kāminī vāsudevasya anumate prāptā ca eva kirīṭinā haraṇam gṛhya saṃprāpte kṛṣṇe devakī nandane śakraprastham mahā bāhuḥ prītyā paramayā yutaḥ saṃprāptiḥ cakra dhanuṣoḥ khāṇḍavasya ca dāhanam draupadyāḥ tanayānām ca saṃbhavaḥ atra eva kīrtitaḥ vihāra artham ca gatayoḥ kṛṣṇayoḥ yamunām anu mahā ṛṣeḥ mandapālasya tanaya saṃbhavaḥ adhyāyānām śate dve tu saṃkhyāte parama ṛṣiṇā aṣṭādaśa eva ca adhyāyāḥ vyāsena uttama tejasā sapta śloka sahasrāṇi tathā nava śatāni ca ślokāḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ granthaḥ mahātmanā sabhā kriyā pāṇḍavānām kiṃkarāṇām ca darśanam lokapāla sabhā ākhyānam nāradāt devadarśanāt girivraje niruddhānām rājñām kṛṣṇena mokṣaṇam tathā digvijayaḥ atra eva pāṇḍavānām prakīrtitaḥ rājñām āgamanam ca eva sārhaṇānām mahā kratau rājasūye argha saṃvāde śiśupāla vadhaḥ tathā yajñe vibhūtim tām dṛṣṭvā duḥkha amarṣa anvitasya ca yatra dyūta arṇave magnān draupadī nauḥ iva arṇavāt dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ mahā prājñaḥ snuṣām parama duḥkhitām tārayām āsa tān tīrṇān jñātvā duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ punar eva tatas dyūte samāhvayata pāṇḍavān jitvā ca vana vāsāya preṣayām āsa tān tatas etat sarvam sabhāparva samākhyātam mahātmanā adhyāyāḥ saptatiḥ jñeyāḥ tathā dvau ca atra saṃkhyayā ślokānām dve sahasre tu pañca śloka śatāni ca ślokāḥ ca ekādaśa jñeyāḥ parvaṇi asmin prakīrtitāḥ atas param tṛtīyam tu jñeyam āraṇyakam mahat vana vāsam prayāteṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu anna oṣadhīnām ca kṛte pāṇḍavena mahātmanā dvijānām bharaṇa artham ca kṛtam ārādhanam raveḥ hitam ca bruvataḥ kṣattuḥ parityāgaḥ ambikāsutāt tyaktasya pāṇḍu putrāṇām samīpa gamanam tathā punarāgamanam ca eva dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt karṇa protsāhanam ca eva dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥ tam duṣṭa bhāvam vijñāya vyāsasya āgamanam drutam maitreya āgamanam ca atra rājñaḥ ca eva anuśāsanam dhaumya upadeśāt tigmāṃśu prasādāt anna sambhavaḥ vṛṣṇīnām āgamaḥ yatra pāñcālānām ca sarvaśas śrutvā śakuninā dyūte nikṛtyā nirjitān ca tān kruddhasya anupraśamanam hareḥ ca eva kirīṭinā paridevanam ca pāñcālyāḥ vāsudevasya saṃnidhau āśvāsanam ca kṛṣṇena duḥkha ārtāyāḥ prakīrtitam bāndhava āgamanam ca eva draupadyāḥ ca aśru mokṣaṇam tat kirmīra vadha ākhyānam vṛṣṇīnām āgamaḥ tathā pāñcālānām ca sarveṣām saubha ākhyānam tathā eva ca subhadrāyāḥ sa putrāyāḥ kṛṣṇena dvārakām purīm nayanam draupadeyānām dhṛṣṭadyumnena ca eva hi praveśaḥ pāṇḍaveyānām ramye dvaitavane tatas dharmarājasya ca atra eva saṃvādaḥ kṛṣṇayā saha saṃvādaḥ ca tathā rājñā bhīmasya api prakīrtitaḥ samīpam pāṇḍu putrāṇām vyāsasya āgamanam tathā pratismṛtya atha vidyāyāḥ dānam rājñaḥ mahā ṛṣiṇā gamanam kāmyakam ca api vyāse pratigate tatas darśanam lokapālānām svarga ārohaṇam eva ca yatra cintā samutpannā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya bhūyasī darśanam bṛhadaśvasya mahā ṛṣeḥ bhāvitātmanaḥ tathā akṣahṛdaya prāptiḥ tasmāt eva mahā ṛṣeḥ lomaśasya āgamaḥ ca atra svargāt pāṇḍu sutān prati vana vāsa gatānām ca pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām saṃdeśāt arjunasya atra tīrtha abhigamana kriyā tīrthānām ca phala prāptiḥ puṇya tva ca api kīrtay pulastyatīrtha yātrā ca nāradena mahā ṛṣiṇā tīrtha yātrā tathā eva atra pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām yatra mandāra puṣpa artham nalinīm tām adharṣayat yakṣaiḥ ca api mahā vīryaiḥ maṇimat pramukhaiḥ tathā āgastyam api ca ākhyānam yatra vātāpi bhakṣaṇam indraḥ agniḥ yatra dharmaḥ ca ajijñāsān śibim nṛpam indraḥ śyenaḥ kapotaḥ agniḥ bhūtvā yajñe abhijagmatuḥ ṛśyaśṛṅgasya caritam kaumāra brahmacāriṇaḥ śaryāti yajñe nāsatyau kṛtavān soma pīthinau vijitya sāgaram prāptam pitaram labdhavan ṛṣiḥ pūrvam prakṣiptam aśṛṇot pitaram lavaṇāmbhasi ghoṣa yātrā ca gandharvaiḥ yatra yuddham kirīṭinaḥ punarāgamanam ca eva teṣām dvaitavanam saraḥ jayadrathena apahāraḥ draupadyāḥ ca āśrama antarāt mārkaṇḍeya samasyāyām upākhyānāni bhāgaśas saṃdarśanam ca kṛṣṇasya saṃvādaḥ ca eva satyayā karṇasya parimoṣaḥ atra kuṇḍalābhyām puraṃdarāt tathā yajña vibhūtiḥ ca gayasya atra prakīrtitā āgastyam api ca ākhyānam yatra vātāpi bhakṣaṇam ṛśyaśṛṅgasya caritam kaumāra brahmacāriṇaḥ prabhāsa tīrthe pāṇḍūnām vṛṣṇibhiḥ ca samāgamaḥ śaryāti yajñe nāsatyau kṛtavān soma pīthinau māndhātuḥ ca api upākhyānam rājñaḥ atra eva prakīrtitam indraḥ agniḥ yatra dharmaḥ ca ajijñāsān śibim nṛpam aṣṭāvakrīyam atra eva vivādaḥ yatra bandinā naiyāyikānām mukhyena varuṇasya ātmajena hi vijitya sāgaram prāptam pitaram labdhavan ṛṣiḥ gandhamādana yātrā ca vāsaḥ nārāyaṇa āśrame vrajan pathini mahā bāhuḥ dṛṣṭavan pavanātmajam kadalīkhaṇḍa madhya stham hanumantam mahā balam yatra mandāra puṣpa artham nalinīm tām adharṣayat jaṭāsurasya ca vadhaḥ rākṣasasya vṛkodarāt vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ca rājarṣeḥ tatas abhigamanam smṛtam ārṣṭiṣeṇa āśrame ca eṣām gamanam vāse eva ca protsāhanam ca pāñcālyāḥ bhīmasya atra mahātmanaḥ kailāsa ārohaṇam proktam yatra yakṣaiḥ bala utkaṭaiḥ samāgamaḥ ca pāṇḍūnām yatra vaiśravaṇena ca paulomaiḥ kālakeyaiḥ ca yatra yuddham kirīṭinaḥ vadhaḥ ca eṣām samākhyātaḥ rājñaḥ tena eva dhīmatā pārthasya pratiṣedhaḥ ca nāradena mahā ṛṣiṇā avarohaṇam punar ca eva pāṇḍūnām gandhamādanāt bhīmasya grahaṇam ca atra parvata ābhoga varṣmaṇā amokṣayat yatra ca enam praśnān uktvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kāmyaka āgamanam ca eva punar teṣām mahātmanām tatrasthān ca punar draṣṭum pāṇḍavān puruṣa ṛṣabhān mārkaṇḍeya samasyāyām upākhyānāni sarvaśas pṛthoḥ vainyasya ca ākhyānam yatra uktam parama ṛṣiṇā saṃvādaḥ ca sarasvatyāḥ tārkṣya ṛṣeḥ su mahātmanaḥ mārkaṇḍeya samasyā ca purāṇam parikīrtyate pativratāyāḥ ca ākhyānam tathā eva āṅgirasam smṛtam draupadyāḥ kīrtitaḥ ca atra saṃvādaḥ satyabhāmayā punar dvaitavanam ca eva pāṇḍavāḥ samupāgatāḥ hriyamāṇaḥ tu manda ātmā mokṣitaḥ asau kirīṭinā jayadrathena apaharaḥ draupadyāḥ ca āśrama antarāt cakre ca enam pañcaśikham yatra bhīmaḥ mahā balaḥ sāvitryāḥ ca api upākhyānam atra eva parikīrtyate mārkaṇḍeyasya ca tathā deva ṛṣeḥ nāradasya ca karṇasya parimoṣaḥ atra kuṇḍalābhyām puraṃdarāt yatra asya śaktim tuṣṭaḥ adāt eka vīra vadhāya ca āraṇeyam upākhyānam yatra dharmaḥ anvaśāt sutam jagmuḥ labdha varāḥ yatra pāṇḍavāḥ paścimām diśam etat āraṇyakam parva tṛtīyam parikīrtitam atra adhyāya śate dve tu saṃkhyāte parama ṛṣiṇā ekonasaptatiḥ ca eva tathā adhyāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ekādaśa sahasrāṇi ślokānām ṣaṣ śatāni ca catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ tathā ślokāḥ parva etat parikīrtitam virāṭa nagaram gatvā śmaśāne vipulām śamīm dṛṣṭvā saṃnidadhuḥ tatra pāṇḍavāḥ āyudhāni uta pāñcālīm prārthayānasya kāma upahata cetasaḥ pāṇḍava anveṣaṇa artham ca rājñaḥ duryodhanasya ca cārāḥ prasthāpitāḥ ca atra nipuṇāḥ sarvatas diśam na ca pravṛttiḥ taiḥ labdhā pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām gograhaḥ ca virāṭasya trigartaiḥ prathamam kṛtaḥ hriyamāṇaḥ ca yatra asau bhīmasenena mokṣitaḥ pratyāhṛtam go dhanam ca vikrameṇa kirīṭinā go dhanam ca virāṭasya mokṣitam yatra pāṇḍavaiḥ virāṭena uttarā dattā snuṣā yatra kirīṭinaḥ atra api parisaṃkhyātam adhyāyānām mahātmanā saptaṣaṣṭiḥ atho pūrṇā śloka agram api me śṛṇu ślokānām dve sahasre tu ślokāḥ pañcāśat eva tu parvaṇi asmin samākhyātāḥ saṃkhyayā parama ṛṣiṇā udyogaparva vijñeyam pañcamam śṛṇu atas param upaplavye niviṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu jigīṣayā iti ukte vacane kṛṣṇaḥ yatra uvāca mahāmatiḥ ayudhyamānam ātmānam mantriṇam puruṣa ṛṣabhau akṣauhiṇīm vā sainyasya kasya vā kim dadāmi aham ayudhyamānam sacivam vavre kṛṣṇam dhanaṃjayaḥ madra rājam ca rājānam āyāntam pāṇḍavān prati vara dam tam varam vavre sāhāyyam kriyatām mama śalyaḥ tasmai pratiśrutya jagāma uddiśya pāṇḍavān purohita preṣaṇam ca pāṇḍavaiḥ kauravān prati saṃjayam preṣayām āsa śama artham pāṇḍavān prati yatra dūtam mahā rājaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ pratāpavān śrutvā ca pāṇḍavān yatra vāsudeva purogamān prajāgaraḥ saṃprajajñe dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cintayā śrāvayām āsa rājānam dhṛtarāṣṭram manīṣiṇam manaḥ tāpa anvitaḥ rājā śrāvitaḥ śoka lālasaḥ yatra kṛṣṇaḥ dayā āpannaḥ saṃdhim icchan mahā yaśāḥ svayam āgāt śamam kartum nagaram nāgasāhvayam pratyākhyānam ca kṛṣṇasya rājñā duryodhanena vai vara anveṣaṇam atra eva mātaleḥ ca mahātmanaḥ mahā ṛṣeḥ ca api kathitam caritam gālavasya ca vidulāyāḥ ca putrasya proktam ca api anuśāsanam karṇa duryodhana ādīnām duṣṭam vijñāya mantritam yoga īśvara tvam kṛṣṇena yatra rājsu darśitam upāya pūrvam śauṇḍīryāt pratyākhyātaḥ ca tena saḥ śveta abhiṣekaḥ kṛṣṇa uktaḥ vicitraḥ bahu vistaraḥ pāṇḍavānām yathāvṛttam sarvam ākhyātavan hariḥ sāṃgrāmikam tatas sarvam sajjam cakruḥ paraṃtapāḥ tatas ca api abhiniryātrā ratha aśva nara dantinām yatra rājñā ulūkasya preṣaṇam pāṇḍavān prati śvas bhāvini mahā yuddhe dūtyena krūra vādinā parivādaḥ ca pāṇḍūnām śvas darśana vilambanam ambā upākhyānam atra eva rāma bhīṣma samāgame etad su bahu vṛttānta pañcama parvan bhārata adhyāyāḥ saṃkhyayā tu atra ṣaḍaśīti śatam smṛtam ślokānām ṣaṣ sahasrāṇi tāvanti eva śatāni ca ślokāḥ ca navatiḥ proktāḥ tathā eva aṣṭau mahātmanā vyāsena udāra matinā parvaṇi asmin tapodhanāḥ atas ūrdhvam vicitra artham bhīṣmaparva pracakṣate jambūkhaṇḍa vinirmāṇam yatra uktam saṃjayena ha yatra yuddham abhūt ghoram daśa ahāni ati dāruṇam kaśmalam yatra pārthasya vāsudevaḥ mahāmatiḥ moha jam nāśayām āsa hetubhiḥ mokṣa darśanaiḥ samīkṣya adhokṣajaḥ kṣipram yudhiṣṭhira hite rataḥ rathāt āplutya vegena svayam kṛṣṇaḥ udāra dhīḥ pratoda pāṇiḥ ādhāvat bhīṣmam hantum vyapeta bhīḥ vākya pratoda abhihataḥ yatra kṛṣṇena pāṇḍavaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvā samare sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ śikhaṇḍinam puraskṛtya yatra pārthaḥ mahā dhanuḥ vinighnan niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ rathāt bhīṣmam apātayat ṣaṣṭham etat mahā parva bhārate parikīrtitam adhyāyānām śatam proktam saptadaśa tathā apare pañca śloka sahasrāṇi saṃkhyayā aṣṭau śatāni ca śloka ca catura aśītiḥ parvan asmin prakīrtitāḥ vyāsena veda vidvasā saṃkhyātāḥ bhīṣmaparvaṇi saināpatye abhiṣiktaḥ atha yatra ācāryaḥ pratāpavān grahaṇam dharmarājasya pāṇḍu putrasya dhīmataḥ yatra saṃśaptakāḥ pārtham apaninyuḥ raṇa ajirāt supratīkena nāgena saha śastaḥ kirīṭinā akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta hatvā hataḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ yatra bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ anveṣaṇa artham pārthasya yudhiṣṭhira nṛpa ājñayā praviṣṭau bhāratīm senām apradhṛṣyām suraiḥ api saṃśaptaka avaśeṣam ca kṛtam niḥśeṣam āhave saṃśaptakānām vīrāṇām koṭayaḥ nava mahātmanām kirīṭinā abhiniṣkramya gamitāḥ yama sādanam saṃśaptaka vadha utsāhī jiṣṇuḥ putra vadha arditaḥ pratijñām mahatīm kṛtvā tīrṇaḥ śrīpati māyayā alambuṣaḥ śrutāyuḥ ca jalasaṃdhaḥ ca vīryavān dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāḥ ca tathā pāṣāṇa yodhinaḥ nārāyaṇāḥ ca gopālāḥ samare citra yodhinaḥ ghaṭotkaca ādayaḥ ca anye nihatāḥ droṇaparvaṇi aśvatthāmā api ca atra eva droṇe yudhi nipātite astram prāduścakāra ugram nārāyaṇam amarṣitaḥ vyāsasya ca api āgamanam māhātmyam kṛṣṇa pārthayoḥ śatarudrīyam atra eva śaṃkarasya mahā stavaḥ atra te pṛthivīpālāḥ prāyaśas nidhanam gam droṇaparvaṇi ye śūrāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ adhyāyānām śatam proktam adhyāyāḥ saptatiḥ tathā aṣṭau śloka sahasrāṇi tathā nava śatāni ca ślokāḥ nava tathā eva atra saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśiṇā pārāśaryeṇa muninā saṃcintya droṇaparvaṇi ākhyātam yatra paurāṇam tripurasya nipātanam prayāṇe paruṣaḥ ca atra saṃvādaḥ karṇa śalyayoḥ haṃsakākīyam ākhyānam atra eva ākṣepa saṃhitam vadhaḥ pāṇḍyasya ca tathā aśvatthāmnā mahātmanā saṃśayam gamitaḥ yuddhe miṣatām sarva dhanvinām pratijñā pūrvakam ca api vakṣaḥ duḥśāsanasya ca duḥśāsanasya ca vadhaḥ vṛṣasenasya ca ubhayayoḥ karṇa putraḥ ca pārthena hataḥ karṇasya paśyataḥ yathāvat bala sainyam ca varṇayām āsa vāyujaḥ pūrayitvā añjalim pūrṇām na dadhnaḥ hi īdṛśaḥ rasaḥ anyeṣām ca rasānām tu pratijñā dṛḍha niścayaḥ śāpena eva ca karṇasya tatas cakram mahī gatam nāga mātram valīkam ca karṇaḥ amuñcata phālgune tad bhayāt keśavaḥ bhūmim prāveśayata tam ratham aṣṭamam parva nirdiṣṭam etat bhārata cintakaiḥ ekonasaptatiḥ proktāḥ adhyāyāḥ karṇaparvaṇi catvāri eva sahasrāṇi nava śloka śatāni ca catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ tathā ślokā parva etat parikīrtitam vṛttāni ratha yuddhāni kīrtyante yatra bhāgaśas vināśaḥ kuru mukhyānām śalyaparvaṇi kīrtyate śalyasya nidhanam ca atra dharmarājāt mahā rathāt sainye ca hata bhūyiṣṭhe kiṃcid śiṣṭe suyodhanaḥ hradāt samutthitaḥ yatra dhārtarāṣṭraḥ ati amarṣaṇaḥ bhīmena gadayā yuddham yatra asau kṛtavan saha ūrū bhagnau prasahya ājau gadayā bhīma vegayā sarasvatyāḥ ca tīrthānām puṇya tā parikīrtitā ekonaṣaṣṭiḥ adhyāyāḥ tatra saṃkhyā viśāradaiḥ saṃkhyā bahu vṛttāntā śloka agra ca atra śaṃs trīṇi śloka sahasrāṇi dve śate viṃśatiḥ tathā muninā saṃpraṇītāni kauravāṇām yaśaḥ bhṛtām atas param pravakṣyāmi sauptikam parva dāruṇam vyapayāteṣu pārtheṣu trayaḥ te abhyāyayuḥ rathāḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ sāyāhne rudhira ukṣitāḥ sametya dadṛśuḥ bhūmau patitam raṇa mūrdhani a hatvā sarva pāñcālān dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamān pāṇḍavān ca saha amātyān na vimokṣyāmi daṃśanam tatas kākān bahūn rātrau dṛṣṭvā ulūkena hiṃsitān pāñcālānām prasuptānām vadham prati manaḥ dadhe gatvā ca śibira dvāri durdarśam tatra rākṣasam tena vyāghātam astrāṇām kriyamāṇam avekṣya ca drauṇiḥ yatra virūpākṣam rudram ārādhya sa tvaraḥ prasuptān niśi viśvastān yatra te puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ pāñcālān sa parīvārān jaghnuḥ drauṇi purogamāḥ kṛtavarmaṇā ca sahitaḥ kṛpeṇa ca nijaghnivān yatra amucyanta pārthāḥ te pañca kṛṣṇa bala āśrayāt sātyakiḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ śeṣāḥ ca nidhanam gatāḥ pāñcālānām prasuptānām yatra droṇa sutāt vadhaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya sūtena pāṇḍaveṣu niveditaḥ draupadī putra śoka ārtā pitṛ bhrātṛ vadha arditā kṛta anaśana saṃkalpā yatra bhartṝn upāviśat priyam tasyāḥ cikīrṣan vai gadām ādāya vīryavān a pāṇḍavāya iti ruṣā drauṇiḥ astram avāsṛjat mā evam iti abravīt kṛṣṇaḥ śamayan tasya tat vacaḥ drauṇeḥ ca droha buddhi tvam vīkṣya pāpa ātmanaḥ tathā drauṇi dvaipāyana ādīnām śāpāḥ ca anyonya kāritāḥ maṇim tathā samādāya droṇaputrāt mahā rathāt pāṇḍavāḥ pradaduḥ hṛṣ draupadyai jita kāśinaḥ toyakarmaṇi sarveṣām rājñām udakadānike guh utpad ca ākhyānam karṇasya pṛthā ātman aṣṭādaśā asmin adhyāyāḥ parvaṇi uktāḥ mahātmanā śloka agram atra kathitam śatāni aṣṭau tathā eva ca ślokāḥ ca saptatiḥ proktāḥ yathāvat abhisaṃkhyayā putra śoka abhisaṃtaptaḥ prajñācakṣūḥ narādhipa kṛṣṇa upanītām yatra asau āyasīm pratimām dṛḍhām tathā śoka agni taptasya dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥ saṃsāra gamanam buddhyā hetubhiḥ mokṣa darśanaiḥ vidureṇa ca yatra asya rājñaḥ āśvāsanam kṛtam dhṛtarāṣṭrasya ca atra eva kaurava āyodhanam tathā vilāpaḥ vīra patnīnām yatra ati karuṇaḥ smṛtaḥ krodha āveśaḥ prasādaḥ ca gāndhārī dhṛtarāṣṭrayoḥ yatra tān kṣatriyān śūrān diṣṭāntān anivartinaḥ putrān bhrātṝn pitṝn ca eva dadṛśuḥ nihatān raṇe gāndhāryāḥ ca api kṛṣṇena krodha upaśamana kriyā yatra rājā mahā prājñaḥ sarva dharma bhṛtām varaḥ rājñām tāni śarīrāṇi dāhayām āsa śāstrataḥ etat ekādaśam proktam parva ati karuṇam mahat saptaviṃśatiḥ adhyāyāḥ parvaṇi asmin udāhṛtāḥ ślokāḥ saptaśatam ca atra pañcasaptatiḥ ucyate saṃkhyayā bhārata ākhyānam kartrā hi atra mahātmanā atas param śāntiparva dvādaśam buddhi vardhanam ghātayitvā pitṝn bhrātṝn putrān saṃbandhi bāndhavān śāntiparvaṇi dharmāḥ ca vyākhyātāḥ śaratalpikāḥ āpad dharmāḥ ca tatra eva kāla hetu pradarśakāḥ yān buddhvā puruṣaḥ samyak sarvajña tvam avāpnuyāt mokṣa dharmāḥ ca kathitāḥ vicitrāḥ bahu vistarāḥ dvādaśam parva nirdiṣṭam etat prājña jana priyam parvaṇi atra parijñeyam adhyāyānām śata trayam triṃśat ca eva tathā adhyāyāḥ nava ca eva tapodhanāḥ ślokānām tu sahasrāṇi kīrtitāni caturdaśa pañca ca eva śatāni āhuḥ pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā atas ūrdhvam tu vijñeyam uttamam bhīṣmāt bhāgīrathī putrāt kururājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vividhānām ca dānānām phala yogāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ tathā pātra viśeṣāḥ ca dānānām ca paraḥ vidhiḥ mahābhāgyam gavām ca eva brāhmaṇānām tathā eva ca rahasyam ca eva dharmāṇām deśa kāla upasaṃhitam etat su bahu vṛttāntam uttamam ca anuśāsanam bhīṣmasya atra eva saṃprāptiḥ svargasya parikīrtitā adhyāyānām śatam ca atra ṣaṭcatvāriṃśat eva ca ślokānām tu sahasrāṇi ṣaṣ sapta eva śatāni ca suvarṇa kośa saṃprāptiḥ janman ca ukta parikṣit dagdhasya astra agninā pūrvam kṛṣṇāt saṃjīvanam punar caryāyām hayam utsṛṣṭam pāṇḍavasya anugacchataḥ citrāṅgadāyāḥ putreṇa putrikāyāḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃgrāme babhruvāhena saṃśayam ca atra darśitaḥ anugītā tathā proktā samyak bhagavatā punar kathitaḥ śāśvataḥ dharmaḥ kṛṣṇena arjuna saṃnidhau tathā brāhmaṇa gītā ca saṃvādaḥ guru śiṣyayoḥ sudarśanam tathā ākhyānam vaiṣṇavam dharmam eva ca atra adhyāya śatam triṃśat trayaḥ adhyāyāḥ ca śabditāḥ trīṇi śloka sahasrāṇi tāvanti eva śatāni ca viṃśatiḥ ca tathā ślokāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśiṇā tatas parva pañcadaśam smṛtam yatra rājyam parityajya gāndhārī sahitaḥ nṛpaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra āśrama padam viduraḥ ca jagāma ha yam dṛṣṭvā prasthitam sādhvī pṛthā api anuyayau tadā putra rājyam parityajya guru śuśrūṣaṇe ratā yatra rājā hatān putrān pautrān anyān ca pārthivān loka antara gatān vīrān apaśyat punar āgatān ṛṣi prasāda kṛṣṇasya dṛś āścaryam anuttama tyaktvā śokam sa dāraḥ ca siddhim paramakām gataḥ saṃjayaḥ ca mahāmātraḥ vidvān gāvalgaṇiḥ vaśī dadarśa nāradam yatra dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ nāradāt ca eva śuśrāva vṛṣṇīnām kadanam mahat etat āśrama vāsa ākhyam pūrva uktam su mahā adbhutam dvicatvāriṃśat adhyāyāḥ parva etat abhisaṃkhyayā sahasram ekam ślokānām pañca śloka śatāni ca ṣaṭ eva ca tathā ślokāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśiṇā atas param nibodha idam mausalam parva dāruṇam yatra te puruṣa vyāghrāḥ śastra sparśa sahāḥ yudhi brahmadaṇḍa viniṣpiṣ samīpe lavaṇa ambhasaḥ āpāne pāna galitāḥ daivena abhipracoditāḥ yatra sarva kṣayam kṛtvā tau ubhau rāma keśavau na aticakramatuḥ kālam prāptam sarva haram samam yatra arjunaḥ dvāravatīm etya vṛṣṇi vinākṛtām dṛṣṭvā viṣādam agamat parām ca ārtim nara ṛṣabhaḥ sa satkṛtya yadu śreṣṭham mātulam śaurim ātmanaḥ dadarśa yadu vīrāṇām āpāne vaiśasam mahat śarīram vāsudevasya rāmasya ca mahātmanaḥ saṃskāram lambhayām āsa vṛṣṇīnām ca pradhānatas sa vṛddha bālam ādāya dvāravatyāḥ tatas janam dadarśa āpadi kaṣṭāyām gāṇḍīvasya parābhavam sarveṣām ca eva divyānām astrāṇām aprasanna tām nāśam vṛṣṇi kalatrāṇām prabhāvānām anitya tām dṛṣṭvā nirvedam āpannaḥ vyāsa vākya pracoditaḥ dharmarājam samāsādya saṃnyāsam samarocayet iti etat mausalam parva ṣoḍaśam parikīrtitam adhyāya aṣṭau samākhyātāḥ ślokānām ca śata trayam ślokānām viṃśatiḥ ca eva saṃkhyātā tattva darśiṇā mahāprasthānikam tasmāt ūrdhvam saptadaśam smṛtam yatra rājyam parityajya pāṇḍavāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ draupadyā sahitāḥ devyā siddhim paramakām gatāḥ dadau saṃpūjya tat divyam gāṇḍīvam dhanuḥ uttamam yatra bhrātṝn nipatitān draupadīm ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dṛṣṭvā hitvā jagāma eva sarvān anavalokayān atra adhyāyāḥ trayaḥ proktāḥ ślokānām ca śata tathā viṃśatiḥ ca tathā ślokāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśiṇā prāptam deva ratham svargāt na iṣṭavan yatra dharmarāj āroḍhum su mahā prājñaḥ ānṛśaṃsyāt śunā vinā tām asya avicalām jñātvā sthitim dharme mahātmanaḥ śva rūpam yatra tat tyaktvā dharmeṇa asau samanvitaḥ svargam prāptaḥ sa ca tathā yātanā vipulā bhṛśam śuśrāva yatra dharma ātmā bhrātṝṇām karuṇāḥ giraḥ nideśe vartamānānām deśe tatra eva vartatām anudarśitaḥ ca dharmeṇa devarājñā ca pāṇḍavaḥ āplutya ākāśa gaṅgāyām deham tyaktvā sa mānuṣam etat aṣṭādaśam parva proktam vyāsena dhīmatā karṇasya naraka prāptiḥ pramokṣaḥ ca atra kīrtyate samāgamaḥ ca vīrāṇām svarga loke mahātmanām svāni sthānāni ca prāptāḥ yatra te puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ yatra duryodhana ādīnām śriyam dṛś yudhiṣṭhira nirvedam paramam gatvā svargam na akāṅkṣat avyayam devānām vacanāt yatra tanum tyaktvā mahā rathaḥ adhyāyāḥ pañca saṃkhyātāḥ parva etat abhisaṃkhyayā ślokānām dve śate ca eva prasaṃkhyāte tapodhanāḥ nava ślokāḥ tathā eva anye saṃkhyātāḥ parama ṛṣiṇā aṣṭādaśa evam etāni parvāṇi uktāni aśeṣatas harivaṃśaḥ tatas parva purāṇam khila saṃjñitam viṣṇu parva śiśoḥ caryā viṣṇoḥ kaṃsa vadhaḥ tathā bhaviṣyam parva ca api uktam khileṣu eva adbhutam mahat yatra bālye sva karmāṇi ramaṇāni adbhutāni ca anekaiḥ saṃśrayaiḥ ca api jarāsaṃdha vadhena ha vikramāt rukmiṇīm devīm āhṛtya para vīra hā parīkṣya ca nivāsa artham dvārakām viniveśayat rāja śulkām ca vai kṛṣṇaḥ satyabhāmām atha udvahat jitvā amara adhipam yatra pārijātam atha anayat naraka asura kālīya hayagrīvam ca dānavam sahasram ciccheda bāṇasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ naptāram bhāryayā sārdham mumocat yatra saṃyuge bhāratīyā kathā yatra vṛṣṇi vaṃśaḥ ca kīrtyate vārāham nārasiṃham ca vāmanam pauṣkaram tathā jitvā nṛpān rathān tyaktvā bhīmasena bhavat prabhuḥ daśa śloka sahasrāṇi viṃśat śloka śatāni ca khileṣu harivaṃśe ca saṃkhyātāni mahā ṛṣiṇā adhyāyānām sahasram tu kīrtitam vai dvijottamāḥ aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi ślokānām kīrtitāni vai aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi ślokānām ca śatam tathā ślokāḥ ca harivaṃśe prakīrtitāḥ khileṣu harivaṃśasya vyākhyātāḥ parama ṛṣiṇā yatra divyāḥ kathāḥ puṇyāḥ kīrtitāḥ pāpa nāśanāḥ deva asura kathāḥ ca eva vicitrāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ yatra kṛṣṇasya karmāṇi śrūyante janmanā saha adhyāyāḥ tu ekam ekānām saptāśītiḥ udāhṛtā ślokānām ca sahasrāṇi daśa trīṇi śatāni ca pauloma ādīni sarvāṇi daśa aṣṭau ca mahān ṛṣiḥ uktavān sa purāṇāni rahasyam ca avasānikam evam aṣṭādaśa etāni parvāṇi uktāni dhīmatā adhyāyānām sahasre dve parvaṇām śatam eva ca ślokānām ca sahasrāṇi navatiḥ daśa eva ca eṣā vai parvaṇām saṃkhyā ślokāḥ granthe yathākramam yat uktam ṛṣiṇā tena vyāsena uttama tejasā janamejayasya aśvamedham draṣṭu kāmasya dhīmataḥ saṃpravṛttaḥ aśvamedhaḥ ca yatra śakreṇa dharṣitaḥ virodhaḥ ca abhavat rājñaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ tasya ṛtvijaiḥ viśvāvasu pura ānītaḥ rājā rājyam acīkarat eṣā vai parvaṇām saṃkhyā khilāni āha tatas param etat akhilam ākhyātam bhāratam parva saṃgrahāt aṣṭādaśa samājagmuḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ yuyutsayā tat mahat dāruṇam yuddham ahāni aṣṭādaśa abhavat yaḥ vidyāt caturaḥ vedān sāṅga upaniṣadān dvijaḥ na ca ākhyānam idam vidyāt na eva sa syāt vicakṣaṇaḥ artha śāstram idam proktam dharma śāstram idam mahat kāma śāstram idam proktam vyāsena amita buddhinā śrutvā tu idam upākhyānam śrāvyam anyat na rocate puṃskokila rutam śrutvā rūkṣā dhvāṅkṣasya vāc iva evam vijñāya tattva jñāḥ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ bhārata adhyayanāt puṇyāt api pādam adhīyataḥ śraddadhānasya pūyante sarva pāpāni asaṃśayaḥ tribhiḥ varṣaiḥ mahābhāgaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ śubhaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ putram pūrvam adhyāpayat śukam yā kriyā kriyate kā cit yaḥ ca kaḥ cit kriyā vidhiḥ idam pravartate sarvam śrotṝṇām prītaye kṣitau adhīyīta yathānyāyam veda jñaḥ veda bhṛt dvijaḥ na ca asya kavayaḥ ke cid bhaviṣyanti viśeṣaṇe viśeṣaṇe gṛhasthasya trayaḥ eva āśramāḥ yathā dhanyam ārogyam āyuṣyam puṇyam sat karma sādhakam bubhūṣate mahā ākhyānam abhimantavyam āditas yat adhītam tadā samyak dvijaśreṣṭhaiḥ dvijottamāt vaiśaṃpāyana vipra ādyaiḥ taiḥ ca api kathitam tadā asya ākhyānasya viṣaye purāṇam vartate dvijāḥ kriyā guṇānām sarveṣām idam ākhyānam āśrayaḥ indriyāṇām samastānām citrāḥ iva manaḥ kriyāḥ āhāram an apāśritya śarīrasya iva dhāraṇam sādhoḥ iva gṛhasthasya śeṣāḥ trayaḥ iva āśramāḥ arthāḥ striyaḥ ca nipuṇaiḥ api sevyamānā dvaipāyana oṣṭha puṭa niḥsṛtam aprameyam puṇyam pavitram atha pāpa haram śivam ca mahābhāratam ākhyāya saṃdhyām mucyati paścimām yat rātrau kurute pāpam karmaṇā manasā girā mahābhāratam ākhyāya pūrvām saṃdhyām pramucyate yaḥ go śatam kanaka śṛṅga mayam dadāti puṇyām ca bhārata kathām śṛṇuyāt ca nityam śrutvā ādau bhavati nṛṇām sukha avagāham vistīrṇam lavaṇa jalam yathā plavena uvāca janamejayaḥ pārikṣitaḥ saha bhrātṛbhiḥ kurukṣetre dīrgha sattram upāste teṣu tat satram upāsīneṣu tatra śvā abhyāgacchat sārameyaḥ tam mātā rorūyamāṇam uvāca rodiṣi tam mātā pratyuvāca sa tām punar uvāca na aparādhyāmi kim cit na avekṣe havīṃṣi na avalihe iti yasmāt ca ayam abhihataḥ anapakārī tasmāt adṛṣṭam tvām bhayam āgamiṣyati iti sa janamejayaḥ evam uktaḥ devaśunyā saramayā dṛḍham saṃbhrāntaḥ viṣaṇṇaḥ ca āsīt sa kadā cit mṛgayām yā pārikṣitaḥ janamejaya kasmin cit sva viṣaya uddeśa āśramam apaśyat tatra kaḥ cit ṛṣiḥ āsām cakre śrutaśravas nāma tad abhiman putraḥ ās somaśravas nāma sa namaskṛtya tam ṛṣim uvāca mahā tapasvī svādhyāya saṃpannaḥ mad tapaḥ vīrya saṃbhṛ mad śukram pītavatyāḥ tad kukṣi saṃvṛdh samartha ayam bhavat sarva pāpa kṛtyā śamay antareṇa mahādeva kṛtyā sa tam purohitam upādāya upāvṛttaḥ bhrātṝn uvāca mad idam vṛ upādhyāya sa tathā bhrātṝn saṃdiśya takṣaśilām pratyabhipratasthe tam ca deśam vaśe sthāpayām āsa saḥ ekam śiṣyam āruṇim pāñcālyam preṣayām āsa gaccha kedārakhaṇḍam badh iti sa upādhyāya saṃdiś āruṇi pāñcālya tatra gam tad kedārakhaṇḍa bandh na aśak sa kliśyamānaḥ apaśyat upāyam bhavatu evam kṛ iti sa tatra saṃviveśa kedārakhaṇḍe tatas kadā cit upādhyāyaḥ āyodaḥ dhaumyaḥ śiṣyān apṛcchat kva āruṇi pāñcālyaḥ gam iti pratyūcuḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ tān śiṣyān pratyuvāca sa tatra gatvā tasya āhvānāya śabdam cakāra bho āruṇe pāñcālya kva as sa tat śrutvā āruṇiḥ upādhyāya vākyam tasmāt kedārakhaṇḍāt sahasā utthāya tam upādhyāyam upatasthe ayam asmi atra kedārakhaṇḍe niḥsaramāṇam udakam avāraṇīyam saṃroddhum saṃviṣṭaḥ bhagavat śabdam śru eva sahasā vidārya kedārakhaṇḍam bhavantam upasthitaḥ bhavat ka karavāṇi iti tam upādhyāyaḥ abravīt yasmāt bhavat kedārakhaṇḍa avadāray utthā tasmāt bhavat uddālaka eva nāman bhū iti saḥ upādhyāyena anugṛhītaḥ yasmāt tvayā mad vacaḥ anuṣṭhātam tasmāt śreyaḥ avāpsyasi iti sarve ca te vedāḥ pratibhāsyanti sarvāṇi ca dharmaśāstrāṇi iti saḥ evam uktaḥ upādhyāyena iṣṭam deśam jagāma tam upādhyāyaḥ preṣayām āsa saḥ upādhyāya vacanāt arakṣat gāḥ sa ca ahani gāḥ rakṣitvā divasakṣaye abhyāgamya upādhyāyasya agratas sthā namaścakre tam upādhyāyaḥ pīvānam apaśyat pīvān asi dṛḍham iti saḥ upādhyāyam pratyuvāca bhaikṣeṇa vṛttim kalpayāmi iti sa tasmāt upādhyāyaḥ sarvam eva bhaikṣam agṛhṇāt tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca rakṣitvā ca āgam tathā eva upādhyāyasya agratas sthā namaścakre tam upādhyāyaḥ tathā api pīvasam eva dṛṣṭvā uvāca vatsa upamanyo sarvam aśeṣatas te bhaikṣam gṛhṇāmi kena idānīm vṛttim kalpayasi iti tena vṛttim kalpayāmi iti tam upādhyāyaḥ prati vac na eṣā nyāyyā guru vṛttiḥ anyeṣām api vṛtti uparodham karoṣi evam vartamānaḥ rakṣ ca punar upādhyāya gṛha āgam upādhyāya agratas sthā namaskṛ tad upādhyāyaḥ tathā api pīvasam eva dṛṣṭvā punar vac aham te sarvam bhaikṣam gṛhṇāmi na ca anyat carasi asi saḥ upādhyāyam prati vac bho etad go payas vṛtti kalpay iti tad upādhyāyaḥ prati vac tam upādhyāyaḥ pīvasam eva apaśyat bhaikṣam na aśnāsi na ca anyat carasi asi bhoḥ phena pā yad idam vatsa mātṛ stana pā udgṛ iti tam upādhyāyaḥ prati vac tat evam api vatsānām vṛtti uparodham karoṣi evam vartamānaḥ sa tathā iti pratijñāya nirāhāraḥ tāḥ gāḥ arakṣat tathā pratiṣidh bhaikṣam na aśnāti na ca anyat carati sa kadā cit araṇye kṣudhā ārtaḥ arka patrāṇi abhakṣayat sa taiḥ arka pattraiḥ bhakṣitaiḥ kṣāra kaṭu uṣṇa vipākibhiḥ cakṣuṣi upahataḥ andhaḥ abhavat saḥ andhaḥ api caṅkramyamāṇaḥ kūpe apatat na āyāti upamanyuḥ ūcuḥ vanam gataḥ gāḥ rakṣitum iti tān āha upādhyāyaḥ atha tasmin an āgacchati upādhyāyaḥ śiṣyān avocat sa tad āhvānam upādhyāyāt śrutvā pratyuvāca uccais tam upādhyāyaḥ prati vac arka pattrāṇi bhakṣayitvā andhībhūtaḥ asmi tam upādhyāyaḥ prati vac tau tvām cakṣuṣmantam kariṣyataḥ devabhiṣajā iti pra pūrva gau pūrva jau citra bhānū girā vā śaṃsāmi tapanau anantau tāvat su vṛttau anamanta māyayā sattamāḥ gāḥ aruṇāḥ udāvahan ṣaṣṭiḥ ca gāvaḥ tri śatāḥ ca dhenavaḥ ekam vatsam suvate tam duhanti nānā goṣṭhāḥ vihitāḥ eka dohanāḥ tau aśvinau duhataḥ gharmam ukthyam ekām nābhim sapta śatāḥ arāḥ śritāḥ pradhiṣu anyāḥ viṃśatiḥ arpitāḥ arāḥ ekam cakram vartate dvādaśa aram pradhi ṣaṇṇābhim eka akṣam amṛtasya dhāraṇam yasmin devāḥ adhi viśve viṣaktāḥ tau aśvinau muñcataḥ mā viṣīdatam idam vṛttam api varṣāsu bhūyas tirodhattām aśvinau dāsa patnīḥ bhittvā meghān aśivam udācarantam aśvinau indram amṛtam vṛtta bhūyau tirodhattām aśvinau dāsa patnī yuvām diśaḥ janayathaḥ daśa agre samānam mūrdhni rathayāḥ viyanti tāsām yātam ṛṣayaḥ anuprayānti devāḥ manuṣyāḥ kṣitim ācaranti yuvām varṇān vikuruthaḥ viśva rūpān te adhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśvā te bhānavaḥ api anusṛtāḥ caranti devāḥ manuṣyāḥ kṣitim ācaranti tau nāsatyau aśvinau vām srajam ca yām bibhṛthaḥ puṣkarasya tau nāsatyau amṛtau ṛtāvṛdhau ṛte devāḥ tat prapadena sūte cakṣuḥ vihīnaḥ pathini saṃpramūḍhaḥ tvām śaraṇyau śaraṇam prapadye evam tena abhiṣṭutau aśvinau ājagmatuḥ āhatuḥ ca enam svaḥ eṣa te apūpaḥ aśāna enam iti tatas tam aśvinau ūcatuḥ āvayoḥ purastāt bhavat upādhyāya evam eva abhiṣṭu apūpa prī datta tam aśvinau āhatuḥ prī svaḥ te anayā guru vṛttyā upādhyāyasya te kārṣṇāyasāḥ dantāḥ cakṣuṣmān ca bhaviṣyasi śreyaḥ ca avāp iti saḥ evam vac aśvibhyām labdha cakṣuḥ upādhyāya sakāśam āgamya upādhyāyam abhivādya ācakṣ tad ca asya prītimān abhūt yathā aśvin āhatuḥ tathā tvam śreyaḥ avāpsyasi iti eṣā tasya api parīkṣā upamanyoḥ tam upādhyāyaḥ saṃdideśa bhavatā mad gṛhe kaṃ cit kālam śuśrūṣamāṇena bhavitavyam sa tathā iti vaktvā guru kule dīrgha kālam guru śuśrūṣaṇa paraḥ avasat go iva nityam guru dhūrṣu niyuj śīta uṣṇa kṣudh tṛṣṇā duḥkha saha sarvatra a pratikūla tasya mahatā kālena guruḥ paritoṣam jagāma tad paritoṣāt ca śreyaḥ sarvajña tām ca avāp eṣā tasya api parīkṣā vedasya saḥ upādhyāyena anujñātaḥ samāvṛttaḥ tasmāt guru kula vāsāt gṛha āśramam pratyapadyata tasya api sva gṛhe vasataḥ trayaḥ śiṣyāḥ babhūvuḥ sa śiṣyān na kim cit uvāca karma vā kriyatām guru śuśrūṣā vā iti duḥkha abhijñaḥ hi guru kula vāsasya śiṣyān parikleśena yojayitum na iyeṣa atha kasya cit kālasya vedam brāhmaṇam janamejayaḥ pauṣyaḥ ca kṣatriyau upetya upādhyāyam varayām cakratuḥ sa kadā cit yājya kāryeṇa abhiprasthitaḥ uttaṅkam nāma śiṣyam niyojayām āsa saḥ evam pratisamādiśya uttaṅkam vedaḥ pravāsam jagāma sa vasan tatra upādhyāya strībhiḥ sahita āhūya uktaḥ upādhyāyinī te ṛtumatī upādhyāyaḥ ca proṣitaḥ etat viṣīdati iti na mayā strīṇām vacanāt idam akāryam kāryam na hi aham upādhyāyena saṃdiṣṭaḥ tad punar upādhyāyaḥ kāla antara gṛha upajagāma tad pravāsa sa tad vṛttam tasya aśeṣa upalabhya prītimān abhūt uvāca sarvam kṛtam iti pratyuvāca vatsa uttaṅka ka tvad priya kṛ iti dharmataḥ hi śuśrūṣitaḥ asmi bhavatā tena prītiḥ paraspareṇa āvayoḥ saṃvṛddhā ka tvad priya kṛ iti evam hi āhuḥ yad ca adharmeṇa vibrūyāt yad ca adharmeṇa pracch vatsa uttaṅka uṣyatām tāvat iti sa kadā cit tam upādhyāyam āha uttaṅkaḥ bhavat tam upādhyāyaḥ prati vac enām praviśya upādhyāyinīm pṛccha kim upaharāmi iti bhavati upādhyāyena asmi anujñātaḥ gṛham gantum tat icchāmi iṣṭam te guru artham upahṛtya anṛṇaḥ gantum tat ājñāpayatu bhavatī gaccha pauṣyam rājānam tābhyām ābandh brāhmaṇān pariveṣṭum iṣ śobhamāna yathā tad kuṇḍalābhyām tad ahar saṃpāday śreyaḥ hi te syāt kṣaṇam kurvataḥ iti saḥ evam vaktaḥ upādhyāyinyā prātiṣṭhata uttaṅkaḥ sa pathin gam apaśyat ṛṣabham atipramāṇa tam adhirūḍham ca puruṣam atipramāṇam eva tad aha puruṣaḥ bhūyas vicāraya upādhyāya api tvad bhakṣay pūrvam iti tad evam vac bāḍham iti vac tadā tad ṛṣabha purīṣa mūtra ca bhakṣay uttaṅka pratasthe yatra sa kṣatriya pauṣya tam upetya apaśyat uttaṅkaḥ āsīnam kim karavāṇi iti tam uvāca uttaṅkaḥ tasyāḥ tat strīdhanam indreṇa yajñe tuṣṭena dattam āsīt tam pauṣyaḥ prativac praviś antaḥpuram kṣatriyā yācyatām iti sa tad evam ukta praviś antaḥpuram kṣatriyām na apaśyat sa pauṣya punar uvāca na hi te kṣatriyā antaḥpure saṃnihitā na enad paśyāmi iti samprati bhavat ucchiṣ na hi sā kṣatriyā ucchiṣṭena aśucinā vā śakyā draṣṭum pativratā tvāt eṣā na aśuceḥ darśanam upaiti iti as khalu mad ucchiṣṭa upaspṛś śīghram gam ca iti tad pauṣyaḥ prativac atha uttaṅka tathā iti vac prāñc mukha upaviś su prakṣālay pāṇi pāda vadana aśabda hṛdayaṃgama ap upaspṛś tris pā dvis parimṛj kha ap upaspṛś antaḥpura praviś tad kṣatriyā paś tad ca dṛṣṭvā eva uttaṅkam abhyutthāya abhivāday uvāca ājñāpay ka kṛ iti tad tām uvāca etad kuṇḍale takṣaka nāga rāja prārthayati saḥ evam uktaḥ tām kṣatriyām prativac na mām śaktaḥ takṣakaḥ nāga rājaḥ dharṣayitum iti tad evam vac tām kṣatriyām āmantrya pauṣya sakāśa āgam tad tam dṛṣṭvā uvāca bhoḥ pauṣya prī as iti tam pauṣyaḥ prati vac bhagavant cirasya pātra āsāday bhavān ca guṇavān atithi tat kariṣye śrāddham kṣaṇaḥ kri iti kṛtakṣaṇaḥ eva asmi atha uttaṅka śīta anna sa keśa dṛś aśuci etad iti man pauṣya vac dātum tasmāt annam eva pratyakṣīkuru tad pauṣyaḥ prativac yasmāt tvad api aduṣṭa annam dūṣayasi tasmāt anapatya bhū iti tad atha pauṣyaḥ tasya aśuci bhāvam annasya āgamay as atha tat annam mukta keśayā striyā upahṛ sa keśa aśuci man uttaṅkam prasādayām āsa bhagavat ajñāna etad annam sa keśa upahṛ śīta ca na mṛṣā bravīmi tad pauṣyaḥ prativac na aham śaktaḥ śāpam pratyādātum ka ca etad bhavat na jñā yathā nāvanītam hṛdayam brāhmaṇasya vāci kṣuraḥ nihitaḥ tīkṣṇa dhāraḥ viparītam etat ubhayam kṣatriyasya vāc nāvanītī hṛdayam tīkṣṇa dhāram mama śāpaḥ bhaviṣyati iti tad evam gam na śak aham tīkṣṇa hṛdaya tva tad śāpa anyathā kṛ yasmāt aduṣṭa anna dūṣayasi tasmāt anapatyaḥ bhū iti duṣ ca anna na etad mad śāpa bhū iti sādhay tāvat iti vac prasthā uttaṅka tad kuṇḍala grah tad apaśyat pathin nagna śramaṇa āgam muhur muhur dṛś a dṛś ca kṛtvā mahatā javena tam anvayāt tasya takṣakaḥ dṛḍham āsannaḥ sa tam jagrāha etad antara sa śramaṇa tvar upasṛtya te kuṇḍale gṛhītvā pradru sa tat rūpam vihāya takṣaka rūpam kṛtvā sahasā dharaṇyām vivṛtam mahā bilam viveśa atha uttaṅkaḥ tasyāḥ kṣatriyāyāḥ vacaḥ smṛtvā tam takṣakam anvagacchat sa tat bilam daṇḍa kāṣṭhena cakhāna na ca aśakat tam kliśyamānam indraḥ apaśyat sa vajram preṣayām āsa asya brāhmaṇasya sāhāyyam kuruṣva iti atha vajraḥ daṇḍa kāṣṭham anupraviśya uccāvaca krīḍā āścarya sthāna avakīrṇam apaśyat tatra praviśya ca nāgān astuvat ebhiḥ ślokaiḥ ye airāvata rājānaḥ sarpāḥ samiti śobhanāḥ varṣantaḥ iva jīmūtāḥ sa vidyut pavana īritāḥ surūpāḥ ca virūpāḥ ca tathā kalmāṣa kuṇḍalāḥ āditya vat nāka pṛṣṭhe rejuḥ airāvata udbhavāḥ bahūni nāgavartmāni gaṅgāyāḥ tīre uttare icchet kaḥ arka aṃśu senāyām cartum airāvatam vinā śatāni aśītiḥ aṣṭau ca sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ sarpāṇām pragrahāḥ yānti dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ yat ejati aham airāvata jyeṣṭha bhrātṛbhyaḥ akaravam namaḥ yasya vāsaḥ kurukṣetre khāṇḍave ca bhavat sadā tam kādraveyam astauṣam kuṇḍala arthāya takṣakam nadīm mandākinīm ramyām prasanna salilām anu takṣakaḥ ca aśvasenaḥ ca nityam sahacarau ubhau kurukṣetre nivasatām nadīm ikṣumatīm anu nāga rājāya mukhyāya kuṇḍale āpnuyām yathā karavāṇi sadā ca aham namaḥ tasmai mahātmane tadā vai cintayām āsa upādhyāyyā yat īritam kāle ca samatikrānte śāpam dāsyati manyunā tad ca tantra kṛṣṇa sita ca tantu cakra ca apaśyat ṣaṣ kumāra parivartay puruṣam ca apaśyat darśanīyam tad tān sarvān tuṣṭāva idam mantravāda ślokaiḥ trīṇi arpitāni atra śatāni madhye ṣaṣṭiḥ ca nityam carati dhruve asmin kṛṣṇān sitān ca eva vivartayantyau bhūtāni ajasram bhuvanāni ca eva kṛṣṇe vasānaḥ vasane mahātmā satya anṛte yaḥ vivinakti loke yaḥ vājinam garbham apām purāṇam vaiśvānaram vāhanam abhyupetaḥ namaḥ sadā asmai jagat īśvarāya lokatraya īśāya puraṃdarāya tatas tad enad puruṣa prāh ka tvad priya karavāṇi iti nāga mad vaśa i iti tad enad puruṣaḥ punar uvāca atha aśvāt dham sarva srotobhyaḥ sa dhūma arcis agneḥ niṣpat tā nāga lokaḥ dhūpitaḥ atha sa sambhramaḥ takṣakaḥ agni tejaḥ bhaya viṣad te kuṇḍale gṛhītvā sahasā sva bhavanāt niṣkramya uttaṅkam uvāca etad kuṇḍale pratigrah bhavat iti kuṇḍale pratigṛhya acintayat adya tat puṇyakam upādhyāyinyāḥ dūram ca aham abhyāgataḥ eṣa tvām kṣaṇāt eva upādhyāya kula prāpayiṣyati iti upādhyāyinī ca snā keśān āvapay upaviś uttaṅka na āgam iti śāpa asya manaḥ dhā atha uttaṅkaḥ praviśya upādhyāyinīm abhyavādayat te ca asyai kuṇḍale prāyacchat tad ca enam prati vac uttaṅka deśe kāla abhyāgataḥ manāk asi mad na śap tad upādhyāyaḥ prati vac ka ciram kṛ iti tam uttaṅkaḥ upādhyāyam prati vac bhoḥ takṣaka nāga rāja vighna kṛ asmin karman tena asmi nāga lokam nītaḥ tad ca tantra kṛṣṇa sita ca tantu tatra ca mayā cakram dṛṣṭam dvādaśan aram ṣaṭ ca enam kumārāḥ parivartayanti puruṣaḥ ca api mayā dṛṣṭaḥ tad punar ka aśvaḥ ca ati pramāṇa yuktaḥ sa ca api kaḥ pathini gacchatā mayā ṛṣabhaḥ dṛś tam ca puruṣaḥ adhirūḍhaḥ uttaṅka idam ṛṣabhasya purīṣam bhakṣaya ye tvad striyau dhātā vidhātā ca ye ca te kṛṣṇāḥ sitāḥ ca tantavaḥ te rātri ahanī dvādaśa aram dvādaśa māsāḥ yat api tat cakram dvādaśa aram ṣaṭ kumārāḥ parivartayanti te ṛtavaḥ ṣaṣ saṃvatsaraḥ cakram yad puruṣa tad parjanya yaḥ aśvaḥ saḥ agniḥ yad ṛṣabha tvad pathin gam dṛś tad airāvata nāga rāja yad ca enam adhirūḍhaḥ tad indra yat api te purīṣam bhakṣitam tasya ṛṣabhasya tat amṛtam tad anugraha kuṇḍala grah punar abhyāgam as śreyaḥ avāp iti sa upādhyāya anujñā uttaṅka krudh takṣaka praticikīrṣ hāstinapura pratasthā purā takṣaśilātaḥ tam nivṛttam aparājitam samyak vijayinam dṛṣṭvā samantāt mantribhiḥ vṛtam tasmai jaya āśiṣaḥ pūrvam yathānyāyam prayuj saḥ uvāca enam vacaḥ kāle śabda saṃpannayā girā bālyāt iva anyat eva tvam kuruṣe nṛpa sattama āsām prajānām paripālanena svam kṣatra dharmam paripālayāmi prabrūhi vā kim kriyatām dvijendra śuśrūṣuḥ asmi adya vacaḥ tvadīyam saḥ evam uktaḥ tu nṛpa uttamena dvijottamaḥ puṇya kṛtām variṣṭhaḥ uvāca rājānam adīna sattvam svam eva kāryam nṛpateḥ ca yat tat kārya kāla ca man aham vidhi dṛś karman tena hi anaparādhī sa daṣṭaḥ duṣṭa antarātmanā akāryam kṛtavān pāpaḥ yaḥ adaśat pitaram tava rājarṣi vaṃśa goptāram amara pratimam nṛpam jaghāna kāśyapam ca eva nyavartayata pāpa kṛt evam pituḥ ca apacitim gatavan tvam bhaviṣyasi karmaṇaḥ pṛthivīpāla mama yena durātmanā uttaṅka vākya haviṣā dīptaḥ agniḥ haviṣā yathā apṛcchat ca tadā rājā mantriṇaḥ svān su duḥkhitaḥ yadā eva pitaram vṛttam uttaṅkāt aśṛṇot tadā lomaharṣaṇa putra ugraśravas sūta paurāṇika naimiṣa araṇya śaunaka kula pati dvādaśan vārṣika sattra ṛṣi abhyāgam upasthā paurāṇikaḥ purāṇe kṛ śrama sa tad kṛtāñjali uvāca kim aham bruvāṇi iti tam ṛṣayaḥ vac parama lomaharṣaṇa pracch tvad vac ca naḥ śuśrūṣ kathā yoga yaḥ asau divyāḥ kathāḥ veda devatā asura saṃkathāḥ dakṣaḥ dhṛta vrataḥ dhīmān śāstre ca āraṇyake guruḥ sarveṣām eva naḥ mānyaḥ sa tāvat pratipālyatām uvāca tena pṛṣṭaḥ kathāḥ puṇyāḥ vakṣyāmi vividha āśrayāḥ saḥ atha vipra ṛṣabhaḥ kāryam kṛtvā sarvam yathākramam yatra brahmarṣayaḥ siddhāḥ te āsīnāḥ yata vratāḥ yajña āyatanam āśritya sūtaputra puraḥsarāḥ upaviṣṭeṣu upaviṣṭaḥ śaunakaḥ atha abravīt idam uvāca purāṇam akhilam tāta pitā te adhītavan purā bhārata adhyayanam sarvam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt tadā purāṇe hi kathāḥ divyāḥ ādi vaṃśāḥ ca dhīmatām kathyante tāḥ purā asmābhiḥ śrutāḥ pūrvam pituḥ te tatra vaṃśam aham pūrvam śrotum icchāmi bhārgavam kathayasva kathām etām kalyāḥ sma śravaṇe tava uvāca yat adhītam purā samyak dvijaśreṣṭha mahātmabhiḥ vaiśampāyana vipra ādyaiḥ taiḥ ca api kathitam purā tat tāvat śṛṇu yaḥ devaiḥ sa indraiḥ sa agni marut gaṇaiḥ pūjitaḥ pravaraḥ vaṃśaḥ bhṛgūṇām bhṛgu nandana imam vaṃśam aham brahman bhārgavam te mahā mune nigadāmi kathā yuktam purāṇa āśraya saṃyutam śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ brahman purāṇe yat śrutam mayā bhṛguḥ mahā ṛṣiḥ bhagavān brahmaṇā vai svayambhunā varuṇasya kratau jātaḥ pāvakāt iti naḥ śrutam bhṛgoḥ babhūvuḥ ṣaṭ putrāḥ tapasā bhāvitātmanaḥ kaviḥ ca cyavanaḥ ca eva śaṅkhalaḥ ca mahā tapāḥ suraśmiḥ saptaraśmiḥ ca vitathaḥ ca mahā tapāḥ tu putraḥ abhūt ūrvaḥ śrutavatām varaḥ vihavyasya tu dāyādaḥ viharaḥ kīrtimān smṛtaḥ viharasya ātmavān putraḥ vatsaḥ ca adhirathaḥ smṛtaḥ vatsasya api vinindaḥ tu sūnuḥ āsīt mahā tapāḥ vittasya tu mahā tejāḥ babhūva ca śrutaśravāḥ brahma sṛṣṭaḥ mataḥ yena yena pūrvam mahātmanā ṛcīkaḥ tasya tanayaḥ brahma sūnuḥ mahā tapāḥ rumaṇvān ca suṣeṇaḥ ca vasuḥ viśvāvasuḥ tathā tris sapta kṛtvas pṛthivī yena niḥkṣatriyā kṛtā bhṛgoḥ su dayitaḥ putraḥ cyavanaḥ nāma bhārgavaḥ cyavanasya api dāyādaḥ pramatiḥ nāma dhārmikaḥ pramadvarāyām dharma ātmā tava pūrva pitāmahāt uvāca cyavana tvam parikhyātam tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ uvāca bhṛgoḥ su dayitā bhāryā pulomā iti abhiviśrutā tasmin garbhe saṃbhṛte atha pulomāyām bhṛgūdvaha samaye sama śīlinyām dharmapatnyām yaśasvinaḥ abhiṣekāya niṣkrānte bhṛgau dharma bhṛtām vare āśramam tasya rakṣaḥ atha pulomā abhyājagāma ha tam praviśya āśramam dṛṣṭvā bhṛgoḥ bhāryām aninditām hṛcchayena samāviṣṭaḥ vicetāḥ samapadyata abhyāgatam tu tat rakṣaḥ pulomā cāru darśanā tām tu rakṣaḥ tatas brahman hṛcchayena abhipīḍitam dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭam abhūt tatra jihīrṣuḥ tām aninditām jātam iti abravīt kāryam jihīrṣuḥ muditaḥ śubhām sā hi pūrvam vṛtā tena pulomnā tu śuci smitā tām tu prādāt pitā paścāt bhṛgave śāstra vat tadā atha agni śaraṇe apaśyat jvalitam jātavedasam tam apṛcchat tatas rakṣaḥ pāvakam jvalitam tadā śaṃsa me kasya bhāryā iyam agne pṛṣṭaḥ ṛtena vai mayā hi iyam pūrva vṛtā bhāryā arthe varavarṇinī paścāt tu imām pitā prādāt bhṛgave anṛta kāriṇe sā iyam yadi vara ārohā bhṛgoḥ bhāryā rahogatā tathā satyam samākhyāhi jihīrṣāmi āśramāt imām mad purva bhāryām yat imām bhṛguḥ prāpa sumadhyamām a saṃmatam kṛtam mama adya hariṣyāmi āśramāt imām śaṅkamānaḥ bhṛgoḥ bhāryām punar punar apṛcchata sākṣi vat puṇya pāpeṣu satyam brūhi kave vacaḥ mad pūrva bhāryā apahṛtā bhṛguṇā anṛta kāriṇā śrutvā tvattaḥ bhṛgoḥ bhāryām hariṣyāmi aham āśramāt jātavedaḥ paśyataḥ te vada satyām giram mama tasya tat vacanam śrutvā saptārciḥ duḥkhitaḥ bhṛśam satyam vadāmi yadi mama śāpaḥ syāt brahma vittamāt asatyam ced aham brūve patiṣye narakān kramāt bhītaḥ anṛtāt ca śāpāt ca bhṛgoḥ iti abravīt śanais tvayā vṛtā pulomā iyam pūrvam dānava nandana kim tu iyam vidhinā pūrvam mantravat na vṛtā tvayā pitrā tu bhṛgave dattā pulomā iyam yaśasvinī dadāti na pitā te vara lobhāt mahā yaśāḥ atha imām veda dṛṣṭena karmaṇā vidhi pūrvakam bhāryām ṛṣiḥ bhṛguḥ prāpa mām puraskṛtya dānava na anṛtam hi sadā loke pūjyate dānava uttama uvāca agneḥ atha vacaḥ śrutvā tat rakṣaḥ prajahāra tām brahman varāha rūpeṇa manaḥ māruta raṃhasā roṣāt mātuḥ cyutaḥ kukṣeḥ cyavanaḥ tena saḥ abhavat tam dṛṣṭvā mātuḥ udarāt cyutam āditya varcasam sā tam ādāya suśroṇī sasāra bhṛgunandanam cyavanam bhārgavam brahman pulomā duḥkha mūrchitā tām dadarśa svayam brahmā sarva loka pitāmahaḥ rudatīm bāṣpa pūrṇa akṣām bhṛgoḥ bhāryām aninditām sāntvayām āsa bhagavān vadhūm brahmā pitāmahaḥ aśru bindu udbhavā tasyāḥ prāvartata mahā nadī anuvartatī sṛtim tasyāḥ bhṛgoḥ patnyā yaśasvinaḥ tasyāḥ mārgam sṛtavatīm dṛṣṭvā tu saritam tadā nāma tasyāḥ tadā nadyāḥ cakre lokapitāmahaḥ vadhūsarā iti bhagavān cyavanasya āśramam prati saḥ evam cyavanaḥ jajñe bhṛgoḥ putraḥ pratāpavān tam dadarśa pitā tatra cyavanam tām ca bhāminīm sa pulomām tatas bhāryām papraccha kupitaḥ bhṛguḥ na hi tvām veda tat rakṣaḥ mad bhāryām cāru hāsinīm tat tvam ākhyāhi tam hi adya śaptum icchāmi aham ruṣā bibheti kaḥ na śāpāt me kasya ca ayam vyatikramaḥ tatas mām anayat rakṣaḥ krośatīm kurarīm iva sā aham tava sutasya asya tejasā parimokṣitā bhasmībhūtam ca tat rakṣaḥ mām utsṛjya papāta vai uvāca iti śrutvā pulomāyāḥ bhṛguḥ parama manyumān śaśāpa agnim abhikruddhaḥ sarva bhakṣaḥ bhaviṣyasi uvāca śaptaḥ tu bhṛguṇā vahniḥ kruddhaḥ vākyam atha abravīt kim idam sāhasam brahman kṛtavan asi sāṃpratam pṛṣṭaḥ hi sākṣī yaḥ sākṣyam jānamānaḥ anyathā vadet sa pūrvān ātmanaḥ sapta kule hanyāt tathā parān yaḥ ca kārya artha tattva jñaḥ jānamānaḥ na bhāṣate śaktaḥ aham api śaptum tvām mānyāḥ tu brāhmaṇāḥ mama yogena bahudhā ātmānam kṛtvā tiṣṭhāmi mūrtiṣu apaḥ deva gaṇāḥ sarve apaḥ pitṛ gaṇāḥ tathā darśaḥ ca paurṇamāsaḥ ca devānām pitṛbhiḥ saha devatāḥ pitaraḥ tasmāt pitaraḥ ca api devatāḥ ekībhūtāḥ ca pūjyante pṛthaktvena ca parvasu tridaśānām pitṝṇām ca mukham evam aham smṛ amāvāsyām ca pitaraḥ paurṇamāsyām ca devatāḥ sarva bhakṣaḥ katham teṣām bhaviṣyāmi mukham tu aham niroṃkāra vaṣaṭkārāḥ svadhā svāhā vivarjitāḥ vinā agninā prajāḥ sarvāḥ tatas āsan su duḥkhitāḥ agni nāśāt kriyā bhraṃśāt bhrāntāḥ lokāḥ trayaḥ anaghāḥ atha ṛṣayaḥ ca devāḥ ca brahmānam upagamya tu
